Britain Hopes to Reconsider Disarmament 40

(London) Since the news from Rome was published in various newspapers, British officials expect that disarmament talks can be reopened soon. When the disarmament talks are reopened, they will be based on the arms stabilization plan proposed by Italy in January 1934. However, the Italian plan advocates maintaining the status quo of armaments and preserving some combat weapons, which is contrary to Britain's policy of reducing armaments. Therefore, the British side feels very inconvenient. Currently, the situation is observed, depending on the results of French Foreign Minister Laval's visit to Britain. It is generally believed that whether France can participate in British Prime Minister MacDonald's disarmament plan depends on the degree of security guarantees obtained. If France believes that the Rome agreement is sufficient security guarantee, the British side still has to strive to implement the advocacy of reducing armaments. Whether the reduction of armaments can be implemented still depends on whether Germany can return to the League of Nations. In short, this issue will be discussed by Foreign Secretary Simon with Disarmament Conference Chairman Henderson before leaving for Geneva. Henderson will go to Geneva when the League of Nations Executive Council meets to consider the date of the next meeting of the Disarmament Conference Presidium. (Havas dispatch from the 8th)

(London) A cabinet meeting was held today, chaired by Prime Minister MacDonald, to discuss the arms issue. The cabinet believes that whether a general international agreement can be established depends entirely on whether the opinions of Britain and France can be consistent. Therefore, before the two countries jointly study it, they cannot make a decision hastily. As for the various international conventions that have been signed and are in progress, what new hope do they have for the issue of arms limitation? The British government intends to estimate it after consulting the French government before agreeing with Italy and Germany based on accurate principles to start negotiations. However, in the eyes of the British, if the disarmament plan proposed by Prime Minister MacDonald on March 16, 1933, can be reorganized according to the current situation, it will definitely be practical. (Havas dispatch from the 9th)

During the counting of ballots, the Referendum Committee will preside over everything. In addition, representatives of the International Federation, representatives of the French, German, and Saar governments, judges of the Referendum Supreme Court, representatives of various political parties, foreign consuls, and journalists will be invited to the field to visit. Soviet Russian Trains Collide Again, Seven More People Die, Death Toll Reaches Twenty-Three 46

(Moscow) After two trains collided on the Moscow-Leningrad railway trunk line last week, seven more people died from their injuries. The death toll has now reached twenty-three. The number of seriously injured has now been reduced to fifty-six. In addition, there are still some people with minor injuries. It is reported that the accident was caused by the negligence of some workers. For example, the driver of a train ignored the signal to stop, which can be used as evidence. At the same time, the stationmaster at the accident site has been arrested for leaving the station without permission after the accident. (Reuters dispatch from the 9th)

Eighty-Year-Old Man Testifies with Cane in Lindbergh Kidnapping and Murder Case 47

Flemington - The trial of Bruno Richard Hauptmann, a German carpenter accused of kidnapping and murdering Charles Lindbergh Jr., has continued for five days. Today, an eighty-seven-year-old man named Hockemer, walked slowly with his cane to the stand to testify. His testimony was extremely unfavorable to the defendant. The old man spoke in a very low voice, claiming that on the night of March 1, 1932, he saw Hauptmann near the Lindbergh home. Hauptmann was in a car with a ladder inside. The old man pointed at Hauptmann and said, "This is the man." After speaking, he pressed his hand on Hauptmann's shoulder to show that his words were true. Hauptmann appeared calm when he entered the court, but turned pale upon this testimony, only slightly shaking his head to indicate his denial. Another witness, also unfavorable to the defendant, followed. This man, named Perrone, is a streetcar driver. Perrone testified that the defendant gave him one dollar and asked him to deliver a letter to Dr. Condon, who represented Lindbergh in negotiations with the kidnappers after the kidnapping. Perrone approached Hauptmann and placed his hand on his shoulder, saying, "This is the man who asked me to deliver the letter." The defendant's lawyer, Reilly, repeatedly cross-examined this witness, but could not shake his testimony. After leaving the court, Hauptmann told reporters that Perrone was a liar and that he did not know why he would give such testimony, stating he had never met Perrone until Perrone, accompanied by several police officers, entered the police station and falsely claimed to recognize him. The most notable piece of evidence presented in court today was a wooden ladder, said to be the one the kidnappers placed outside the window to enter the house and steal Lindbergh Jr. Fingerprint expert Kelly stated that no fingerprints were found in the Lindbergh house or on the ladder. The defendant's lawyer claimed that Reilly's method of searching for fingerprints had destroyed them, as Kelly used a brush to remove dirt instead of blowing powder. The ladder was disassembled and then reassembled, hence this evidence.

U.S. Treasury Secretary Announces No Change in Silver Purchase Plan, Rumors of Avoiding Raising Silver Prices in China Denied 49

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau today dismissed as a rumor the speculation that the U.S. government, in carrying out its silver purchase program, intends to avoid raising silver prices in the Chinese market. Other Treasury officials told Reuters that the government's silver purchase program is no different from what was stated in the Sino-American exchange of notes in mid-October last year. The U.S. government remains determined to purchase silver on the world market. This policy has been stipulated by congressional legislation and cannot be changed by the executive branch. However, Secretary of State Hull has guaranteed that the United States is willing to avoid disrupting China's economy and finances as much as possible. Reuters has learned that Chinese Ambassador Shih Kung has frequently discussed this matter with Hull since the exchange of notes, but there has been no concrete development. Hull stated on Sunday that he was unaware of any new developments in the silver situation. (Reuters, 8th)

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau told the Associated Press today that the item of silver coinage profits in the government's next budget is of no noteworthy value and does not indicate any change in the silver purchase policy. The budget for the next fiscal year, ending June 30, 1936, lists silver coinage profits at $11.5 million, while the figure for the current fiscal year is $10 million. (National Telegram, 8th)

Conservative Faction Dominates U.S. Congress, Inflationary Policies Difficult to Implement 50

(Washington) In the first week of Congress's session, conservative Democrats have been seen to dominate both houses, making the implementation of inflationary policies unlikely. Future silver and currency legislation will largely conform to the proposals of President Roosevelt and Treasury Secretary Morgenthau. Some compromises may be made if there is strong pressure from the silver bloc. All House leaders, such as Speaker Byrns, Majority Leader Pou, Ways and Means Committee Chairman Doughton, and Rules Committee Chairman O'Connor, are conservatives. In the Senate, besides Vice President Garner as the speaker, others such as Majority Leader Robinson, Banking and Currency Committee Chairman Glass, and Finance Committee Chairman Harrison are also conservatives. While the veterans' bonus issue is generally expected to pass, it remains doubtful whether its implementation will adopt inflationary methods as intended by the original proponents. Today, Representative Fish introduced a compromise bill proposing to pay the bonus in installments but suspend interest payments. If this bill passes, it would require an expenditure of $400 million annually for five years. Fish specifically stated that the payment of this bonus "should not involve increasing taxes or issuing more currency." (National Telegram, 8th)

(Washington) Treasury officials today began planning how to raise $9 billion to meet the needs of President Roosevelt's budget. In the next six months, expenditures are projected at $5 billion, while tax revenues and other income amount to only $1.9 billion, leaving a shortfall of $3.1 billion to be covered by borrowing. In addition, the government's maturing debt reaches $6,291,608,800, so the Treasury's new debt in the next six months may exceed $9 billion. (National Telegram, 8th)

(New York) The revenue from silver coinage tax, as predicted in President Roosevelt's budget message to Congress, is now realized. The estimated revenue from the coinage tax in the fiscal year ending June 30, 1935, is $100 million, and in the 1936 fiscal year, it is $25 million. Therefore, the total revenue from this tax at the end of the 1936 fiscal year will be $125 million. However, this figure is not related to the silver purchase program. (Reuters, 8th)

(Washington) House silver bloc members organized today to promote the coinage of silver in this session of Congress. The group is not divided by party lines and is led by Representative Martin. Both Democratic and Republican members have joined. The House silver bloc plans to consult with Senate silver bloc leaders on cooperative measures, and it is understood that the size and influence of this new organization are superior to those of the silver bloc in the previous Congress. Martin criticized the Treasury's performance in silver purchases today, calling the current silver law like an adopted son of the Treasury. If the Treasury earnestly implemented this law, the price of silver would increase to one dollar per ounce, benefiting miners and inflating the currency. Martin expressed dissatisfaction with the handling of the silver issue and said that the United States currently feels a shortage of currency and relies too much on bank loans. It is said that reducing the gold content of the dollar should be tested by re-coining silver. He added that he personally favors re-coining silver at a ratio of sixteen to one for gold and silver, but silver bloc members have not yet reached a consensus. (National Telegram, 8th)

(Washington) New Deal leaders expressed optimism today, saying that President Roosevelt's $4 billion public works plan could provide jobs for seven million people in 1935, of which 3.5 million would no longer receive government relief and would work for the Public Works Administration. The remaining 3.5 million could be employed by private factories, as commerce is expected to prosper after government encouragement. (National Telegram, 8th)

(Washington) President Roosevelt, suffering from a slight cold, did not go to the office today but handled all important official matters in his private study. (National Telegram, 8th)

Davis Returns to the U.S. and States a New Naval Treaty Could Be Achieved, Submits Opinions to the State Department 51

(Washington) Although the London Naval Conference recently ended without results, U.S. envoy Davis returned to the country today and declared that the London talks had laid the foundation for future agreements, and that an agreement between the U.S., Britain, and Japan might be reached this year. Japan's abrogation of the Washington Naval Treaty should not be seen as the three countries immediately engaging in an arms race, as an arms race is truly unavoidable. In his report submitted to Secretary of State Hull, Davis expressed a conciliatory attitude toward Japan, saying that naval problems could still be solved if countries based their plans on not specifying naval ratios, and that this solution was in line with Britain's views. In principle, all signatory countries could achieve complete equality. (National Telegram, 8th)

(Washington) U.S. representative Davis, returning from Europe, told President Roosevelt that if the spirit of international cooperation is promoted, an agreement on limiting land and naval armaments can be reached within two years. The outline of the British compromise proposal can serve as the best basis for the U.S., Britain, and Japan to limit their navies. The discussions in London have greatly clarified the atmosphere and laid the foundation for future compromise agreements. He expressed optimism about the possibility of a general disarmament agreement in Geneva being reached soon. (Reuters, 8th)

Japan to Reply to Britain, U.S., and Netherlands on the Issue of the Monopoly of Petroleum in the Puppet State 52

(Nanjing) The governments of Britain, the U.S., and the Netherlands have submitted a third protest to the Japanese government regarding the petroleum issue through their respective ambassadors, requesting the Japanese government to provide a detailed explanation. Foreign Minister Hirota plans to issue a formal response to the three countries within this week, explaining that the petroleum monopoly in "Manchukuo" does not violate the principle of the Open Door Policy. (Domei, 9th)

(Nanjing) The governments of Britain, the U.S., and the Netherlands have repeatedly protested to the Japanese government regarding the petroleum monopoly in "Manchukuo." From December 28th to 30th last year, a conference of British and American petroleum companies was held in Shanghai to discuss stopping the sale of British and American petroleum to "Manchukuo." According to information received by a certain office on the 9th, the attendees of the Shanghai petroleum conference were representatives of five petroleum companies: Socony-Vacuum, APC, Texaco, Morgan, and Baudier. The central issue of their discussion was countermeasures to the promotion of Soviet Russian petroleum in the Chinese "Manchukuo" market, aiming to seize the privileges of the Soviet Russian petroleum import merchant, Guanghua Company. They reached agreements on various issues, intending to request the Chinese government to abolish the privileges of Guanghua Company in the future and investigate the sales routes of Russian oil in Manchuria. The plan of the British and American companies to monopolize the petroleum market in the Far East is noteworthy. (Domei, 9th)

Takahashi Urges Cabinet Members to Pay Attention to Investment in Manchuria 53

(Nanjing) At the cabinet meeting on the 8th, Finance Minister Takahashi reminded cabinet members to pay attention to and consider the issue of Manchurian expenses and private investment in Manchuria. This proposal by the Finance Minister aims to control investment in Manchuria and equalize the expenses of the Manchurian Incident. The expenses of the Manchurian Incident have occupied an important position in Japan's international borrowing. Originally, the expenses of the Manchurian Incident were to be equalized starting from the tenth year of Showa (1935) under the then Minister of the Army, Araki, but the budget for the tenth year was still 120 million yen. From this development, future imbalances in international payments will hinder exchange rate policies and have a negative impact on the economic sector. As a result of his concern, the Finance Minister took this action. (Domei, 9th)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance believes that due to changes in Japanese trade and overseas situations, the future of the yen exchange rate will inevitably tend to fall. Therefore, it is suspending the purchase of foreign power bonds and sending cash payments to Manchuria, taking various measures to prevent this. Temporary overseas payments related to the government must also not put pressure on the exchange market. For example, the purchase of the Donglu requires paying 23 million yen in cash, and the result of employee retirement allowances is also to exchange foreign currency in the Japanese market. Therefore, it is asking the Yokohama Specie Bank to seek to increase its foreign currency reserves. Finance Minister Takahashi will invite the authorities of the Yokohama Specie Bank and the Bank of Japan in the next few days to discuss everything.

(Nanjing) News from the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission: Huang Musong has completed his inspection of Nepal and took a ship northward from the Indian capital on the 3rd of this month. He is expected to arrive in Hong Kong on the 17th and return to Nanjing on the 22nd. His entourage of more than ten people, including Gao Changzhu, left India by ship on the 31st of last month and are expected to arrive in Shanghai in about twenty days. (Special Dispatch, 9th)

(Special Dispatch, 9th)

Xu Shiying Discusses the Situation of Relief Efforts 63

(Nanjing) Xu Shiying arrived in Nanjing on the 9th to participate in the Huangshan Construction Committee and handle the affairs of the Relief Association. He will return to Shanghai after meeting with President Wang. According to him, the disaster situation in various provinces last year was severe. After discussing with Finance Minister Kong in Shanghai, the Famine Relief Association of Various Provinces was organized in Shanghai and raised 1,025,000 yuan, which have been distributed to various provinces one after another. However, it is a drop in the bucket and does not solve the problem. It is still necessary to continue raising relief funds. Since the 17th year of the Republic (1928), there has been a disaster every year, and every disaster has been severe. I have been in charge of relief affairs and have raised more than 50 million yuan in total. Given the economic panic in our country, it is extremely difficult. Fortunately, Finance Minister Kong has agreed to include the disaster relief reserve fund in the national annual budget from the 24th year of the Republic (1935) onwards. In the future, when relief funds arrive in Shanghai, they will no longer have to rely entirely on donations. (Central News Agency, 9th)

Wang Yingyu to Go to Gansu in One Month 64

(Nanjing) Wang Yingyu said that after meeting with Chairman Chiang to request instructions, he would go to Gansu to take up his new position as the Director of the Civil Affairs Department. (Central News Agency, 9th)

International Commercial Telegraph

—Special Commercial Report from Reuters on January 9th—

Gold and Silver 76

British Gold: The London gold price today was 141 shillings and 11 pence, down 1 pence.

British Silver: In the London silver market, the United States and speculators bought in, and there were few sellers. Therefore, the silver price rose by 25 today. The spot price is 24 pence and 5625, and the futures price is 24 pence and 6875. The market situation at the close was stable.

Indian Silver: In the Bombay silver market, the spot price rose by 6 annas today. The market sentiment at the close was stable. The price was 6 rupees and 11 annas. The transaction volume was 15 bars. U.S. Silver: The Mountri silver market futures rose by about 30 pounds because the London silver market price rose.

Exchange Rates 77

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was calm this morning, with minimal fluctuations. The British-American exchange rate opened at 4 dollars, 91 and 125 cents, the same as the American-British closing price yesterday. At 11:00, it fell by 0625. At 2:00 PM, it rose by 2 cents, reaching 4 dollars, 91 and 3125 cents.

British-French: The opening price rose by 7 pounds, reaching 74 francs 28. At 11:00, it jumped by 3 pounds. At noon, it jumped by another 4 pounds. But at 2:00 PM, it rose by 7 pounds, restoring the price of 74 francs 28 at the opening.

Cotton and Wheat 78

U.S. Cotton: The New York cotton market opened up 23 points due to purchases from Bombay. The government is no longer selling, so the cotton price is looking good.

Indian Cotton: The Bombay cotton market initially rose due to purchases by cotton merchants, but then fell due to sales by Japanese merchants. The price of Bai Luozhi cotton for the April-May term reached 246 rupees. The closing price fell to 244 rupees and 75, which is still 5 rupees higher than yesterday's closing.

British Cotton: In the Liverpool cotton market, the price for the May term was 6.89 at 1:00 PM, up 3 points.

British Wheat: In the Liverpool wheat market, the price for the May term was 5 shillings and 2 pence and 25 at 1:00 PM, up 375.

U.S. Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened with a downward trend, but the drop was limited. It is reported that the climate in the wheat region is overcast and humid, and colder weather is expected.

Rubber 79

London: The London rubber market situation is quiet. At noon, the trading price for the April-June term was 6 pence and 875, the same as yesterday's price.

New York: The New York rubber market opened sharply down. Although the London market situation is still stable, the price here fell by 11 points.

Securities 80

New York: Before the opening of New York securities, the factors favorable to the market situation were: (1) The new oil industry control legislation is expected to be introduced soon to avoid instability in the oil industry. (2) Trade news is still good. Investors are now showing signs of resuming the purchase of common stocks with some capital. The unfavorable factor to the market situation is that the actions of the country have not been clearly known. Therefore, the selective nature of the demand currently existing in the securities market may continue. The prices are as follows:

The Yellow River in Changyuan Continues to Rise Unabated 89

All the land collapsed and no area was not flooded. The entire city was in danger of submerging. He earnestly requested the allocation of water pumps to pump water to save the people. Representatives of Postal Institutions Sign a Contract to Undertake Business 123

Yu Xianglin and Huang Zigufrom Tianjin Go to Yuguan

Huitong Transfer Bureau Established in Yuguan

Yu Xianglin, in charge of communications for Tianjin's postal service, and Huang Zigu, manager of the Huitong Transfer Bureau, along with more than ten staff members of the Transfer Bureau, took the Pinghu train to Tianjin early on the 5th. They met with Cao Jianting, the postmaster of the Hebei Postal Administration, at noon to negotiate a contract for the Huitong Transfer Bureau. In the evening, Cao Jianting hosted a banquet at the Penglai Spring in the French Concession to entertain Yu Huang and others. On the 6th, continued negotiations were held, and the contract was agreed upon. It is estimated that it can be signed on the 7th. The content of the contract is that the Transfer Bureau is responsible for transferring letters and remittances in the Hebei and Beiping postal districts. The validity period is one year, and it can be renewed after the expiry date. A deposit of 10,000 yuan is also paid. Huang is in Tianjin to handle this matter.

It is necessary to delay for a day or two. On the morning of the 8th, he went to Yuguan to prepare for the establishment of the Transfer Bureau. Another person was sent to arrange for Gubeikou. On the 10th, it is determined that the transfer of letters can be started as scheduled. Regarding this matter, according to Yu Xianglin, "I came to Tianjin to help Huang Zigu handle postal affairs, and I will follow Huang to Yuguan within days. After the Transfer Bureau is established, I will stay there for about two or three days and then return to Beiping to inspect Gubeikou, and then return to Beiping to contact the Ping Postal Administration. After everything is completed, I will return to my post as the postal director of Shanxi. The postal incident started before April. Gao Zongwu and I, as representatives of the General Post Office of the traffic sector on our side, contacted representatives of the Japanese Kwantung Army. This matter is only an agreement between our postal authorities and the Japanese Kwantung Army, and has absolutely nothing to do with our Ministry of Communications. Our country has never recognized the puppet state, and this principle will not be changed after the opening of postal services. In the future, domestic mail sent to the outside of the pass, all those marked with Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, Rehe and other provinces, will be transferred. If there are any words of a puppet organization, they will be prohibited from being posted." According to Huang Zigu, "I am scheduled to go to Yuguan within days to prepare for the establishment of the Huitong Transfer Bureau. When handling this matter, I heard that the postal issue had been decided, so I applied to the Hebei-Beiping Postal Administration as a retired postal worker to undertake postal and remittance matters inside and outside the pass, and set up the Huitong Transfer Bureau to take charge of it. The Hebei-Beiping Postal Administration approved my request because I am familiar with postal affairs. The only procedure between the two parties is to sign a contract and pay a deposit of 10,000 yuan. In the future, after the postal service is opened, the responsibility of the Transfer Bureau is only to transfer affairs. Letters entering the pass from outside the pass must be affixed with special stamps. The Transfer Bureau is responsible for compensating for the mis-posting of puppet country stamps. For all remittances inside and outside the pass, the Transfer Bureau will extract a 1% commission to be used as this compensation fee and the expenses of the entire bureau. Once things are in order and the mis-posting of fake tickets is reduced, the commission will be reduced as appropriate. The bureau is completely commercial in nature and is completely my personal business. As for employment, in addition to my appointment as manager of the Yuguan General Bureau, a supervisor is also appointed, followed by eight or nine clerks and several laborers. The Gubeikou Branch has one branch manager, two clerks, and several laborers. The contract can be signed tomorrow, and all the documents and equipment used are ready in Tianjin. The transfer of various items will be handled on the 10th."

According to inquiries, the Hebei Postal Administration has decided to send inspectors Hu Xinde and Li Jingxi to Yuguan with Huang Yu to monitor the establishment of the Transfer Bureau. However, there are still doubts here, that is, the issue of mail inspection. We do not discriminate against our compatriots in the occupied Northeast. The mail sent from them should also abolish the inspection procedures. Only the local bureaus at the place of delivery have inspectors stationed to pay attention to suspicious mail at any time. The puppet regime has always prevented our books and newspapers from entering the country. The inspection of letters is very strict to prevent secret communication with the volunteers. Now that the postal service is open, the Japanese side has not clearly proposed restrictions on our books and newspapers being mailed, nor has it set up special inspection agencies. Therefore, after the opening of postal services, the real restriction method is still not clear. Therefore, it is generally concluded that the postal service is open in name, but the inspection is still not abolished in substance. (6th)

Fujian Province Schedules Regular Pacification Meetings 124

Remnant Bandits in Northern Fujian Defeated

Relief Situation in Western Fujian

Fuzhou Correspondence: Jiang Dingwen, the Director of Pacification of Fujian, flew from Zhangzhou to the province on December 23 last year and stayed in the province for two weeks. On the morning of the 3rd of this month, he left the province for Xiamen and Zhangzhou with Chief of Staff Li Jianai. Jiang's two major missions this time were, first, to effectively link military and political affairs to handle post-recovery work, and second, to implement the pacification plan of divided defense in each pacification zone and the cooperation methods of various troops and local teams. After consultation and discussion by Director Jiang, Chairman Chen, and Chiefs of Staff Li and Yu, an implementation outline has been formulated. On the 2nd, Director Jiang and Chairman Chen of the Provincial Government had a final meeting, which did not end until after 2 pm. It is now scheduled that the Provincial Pacification Meeting will be held on the 10th of this month in the Zhangzhou Pacification Commissioner's Office. In addition to the four Pacification Commanders, Wei Lihuang, Liu Heding, Li Yannian, and Wang Jingjiu, each of whom will have proposals for clearing up scattered bandits and local post-affairs work, all military officers above the division commander of the troops formerly under the Eastern Route Bandit Suppression Army Headquarters will also attend. Song Yuanquan, the commander of the puppet Fujian-Jiangxi Military Region, who occupies the junction of Ninghua, Mingxi, and Qingliu counties, including Wucun, Quanshang, Shuixi, Fengxi, Tangchi, Anyuan and other areas, and the puppet independent 12th and 16th Independent Regiments, and the guard company training team, and other bandits with more than 2,000 people, were attacked by the 52nd Division Commander Lu Xingrong, who led his team to suppress them. From the middle of last month to the end of the year, the bandits were defeated. The bandit Song led more than 1,000 remnants to retreat to Guangchang and Shicheng. Local order is gradually being restored. The 52nd Division is now convening teams to carry out a thorough investigation. Lu Xingrong will first lead his team back to Ningcheng after the search near Anyuan is completed to discuss the Qingxiang with the county magistrate.

The relief issue in the recovered area of western Fujian has been handled by Kang Shaozhou, a consultant of the Provincial Relief Council, who has established a resident office in Changting and started working on January 4. The relief policy is also planned as follows: (1) Regarding the issue of medical treatment for the people, two medical teams for the people in western Fujian will be formed. All expenses will be paid by the Department of Civil Affairs on a monthly basis, and the Provincial Relief Council will supply the consumption of medicines. (2) Regarding the issue of work relief, Changting's production is mainly paper, with annual exports of no less than 5 million yuan. The cloth used by the people of the whole county is produced by local cloth factories. When the Communist bandits occupied the towns, the paper factories and cloth factories were destroyed. Since the recovery, the operators have mostly been unable to recover. It is decided that the Council will lend capital to help unemployed workers. Regarding the issue of agricultural relief, after Changting was occupied by bandits, farming tools were confiscated and cattle were slaughtered, resulting in difficulties for refugees returning to their hometowns due to the lack of cattle and tools. It is now decided that the Council will buy cattle and tools and borrow seeds to provide for cultivation. (4) Regarding the issue of emergency relief, in addition to providing fundamental relief to agriculture and industry, there are also unemployed people. It is decided that the Council will establish a poverty-stricken people's loan office to lend a small amount of capital to maintain the lives of several people. The rest of the widows, widowers, orphans, and the lonely will be provided with food rations on a daily basis by the Council establishing several porridge factories to avoid starvation. (5th)

The First Phase of Conscription in Jiangxi Province Have All Joined the Army 125

Security Teams to be Eliminated

Supplemented by Conscription in Succession

Nanchang Communications: In order to realize national conscription, Jiangxi Province began conscription in the 24th year, and the details have been recorded in previous reports. The first phase of conscription was 32 regiments, about 40,000 people. This quota of troops was conscripted from strong men aged 21 to 24 in each county and decided by lottery. Since the establishment of the Provincial Government's Higher Conscription Committee last year to supervise the holding of the Conscription Committee in each county, all procedures were completed by the end of last year, and the strong men in various places had also been drawn out early. According to news from Linchuan and other counties, all conscripted recruits reported to the county government on New Year's Day and joined the army, which was quite enthusiastic. More than 90 officers who have completed training by the Provincial Security Headquarters are serving as middle-level cadres and are being trained in teams by region to become an elite force. However, the Conscription Law stipulates that the active service is six months. After this period expires, another period will be conscripted until all the strong men in the province have completed military service. The existing security teams in each county are mostly recruited, and it has been decided to eliminate them in stages and replace them with conscripts in succession. (6th)

A Review of the World Economy in 1934 by Mu Ouchu 135

There are two different observations of the state of the world economy in 1934: pessimistic and optimistic. The former is due to the fact that the overall world trade is still extremely depressed, and it is not daring to speak of recovery and prosperity. The latter is due to the fact that the domestic economies of various countries have partially recovered. However, in reality, did the world economy in 1934 get rid of the panic that had been worsening for several years and gradually enter a state of prosperity? We believe that the greatest characteristic of the world economy in 1934 was that all countries consistently pursued economic nationalism. Economic nationalism, strictly speaking, is fully colored by isolationism. Because of the prohibition of imports and the promotion of exports, it may appear to have partially recovered in the eyes of various countries, but in the view of the entire world, economic recovery is still in a state of uncertainty. Moreover, the content of economic recovery in various countries is entirely the result of developing military industries and implementing inflationary policies. And both of these are preparations for dealing with war. Therefore, we believe that the current popularity of economic nationalism and the partial recovery of the domestic economy actually contain the crisis of the outbreak of the Second World War. The actual situation of the world economy in 1934 tells us that all the materials are not optimistic. Now, we will try to divide the status into industry, agriculture, finance, the struggle for markets, and unemployment, and make a brief narrative as follows.

According to the League of Nations' report on the world economy, the world's total production in 1934 was on the rise. In April 1934, it not only recovered 95.5% of that of 1928, but also increased significantly compared to 83.2% in 1933.

Development of World Industrial Production (According to the Berlin Institute for Economic Research, 1928 = 100)

Average monthly in 1933 83.2

1934 January 88.7

February 91.0

March 94.5

April 95.5

May 94.1

June 92.8

July 88.8

Even from the perspective of individual countries, it also shows a state of development.

Industrial Production Index of Major Countries (According to the League of Nations Monthly Bulletin)

1928 = 100 United States United Kingdom Germany France Japan

Average in 1932 58.6 86.2 60.5 77.5 110.1

Average in 1933 72.1 90.2 69.0 80.3 134.3

January 1934 70.3 103.3 79.1 83.5 142.5

February 73.6 103.3 82.5 82.7 139.1

March 76.6 103.3 84.2 81.8 139.8

April 77.5 104.1 85.7 81.1 141.3

May 77.5 104.1 88.9 79.5 148.1

June 丨丨丨 104.1 88.5 78.0 丨丨丨

The industrial production indices of the United Kingdom, the United States, and Germany have all exceeded the levels of the previous two years. Especially in Japan, it has surpassed all countries and developed rapidly. Only France has shown signs of decline. This illustrates the difference between being able to adopt an inflationary policy and having to adhere to a deflationary policy. France is known as the world's second largest gold store, and many people rely on interest for their livelihood, so it is not easy to implement an inflationary policy for a while, and the industry has also declined. Therefore, France is now striving to plan the organization of the gold standard group economy, the intention of which is nothing more than to protect the prosperity of its own industry. However, the development of the economies of the UK and the US, which have stopped the gold standard and implemented inflationary policies, is only like this.

UK and US Economic Index

(UK numbers are based on the Economic Magazine survey, 1924 = 100, US numbers are estimated based on the Annali·t survey level) UK US

Average from January to August 1932 95.65 63.8

Same period in 1933 98.49 71.9

Same period in 1934 107.84 76.2

Although the United Kingdom has improved slightly compared to the United States, it is artificial and there is still no amazing development. If the UK and the US are like this, it is even more conceivable what the economic situation in the world is like.

Moreover, the content of the increase in industrial production is mostly the progress of the military industry. Regarding the military industry, because it is the secret of various countries, although there is a lack of accurate statistics, we can prove one aspect of the rapid development of the military industry from the increase in the productivity of the steel industry. The production of world steel has been prosperous since 1933. The increase in the first half of 1934 was even more significant. The steel production of major countries such as the United Kingdom, the United States, Germany, and the Soviet Union is listed as follows:

Country Production Amount First Half of 1933

United States 7,019 3,027 (Unit: Thousand Tons)

Germany 2,570 1,592

United Kingdom 2,249 1,505

Soviet Union 2,116 1,058

Total 13,954 7,182

(According to page 77 of the third issue of the first volume of Cultural Construction)

The annual increase rate of steel reached 41%. The second half of the year even has a greater tendency to increase. Doesn't this indicate that the world is about to face a war crisis? (To be continued)

City News

He Bingxian Visited the French Commercial Counselor Yesterday 136

Inquired About Morocco's Re-imposition of Tea Tax

Counselor Shu Replied That He Fears This Will Not Happen

The Industry Association said that Mr. He Bingxian, Director of the International Trade Bureau, according to the Yangzhuang Tea Trade Association, France intends to re-impose import taxes on Chinese tea in Morocco and other places, and it is scheduled to be implemented on January 1 this year, which will have a significant impact on the future of China's tea industry. He, together with Ji Zejin, Director of the Guidance Department, visited Mr. Shu Xin, Commercial Counselor of the French Consulate General on the Bund of this city at about 9:00 am yesterday for informal talks to inquire in detail about the heavy taxation of Chinese Yangzhuang tea in French Morocco and other places. Mr. Shu replied that French Morocco is an international area, and in fact, it is not something that legal persons can freely and actively control. He has not heard of the imposition of tea tax. Moreover, Annam and other places in the entire territory of this country are tea-producing areas, and the tea produced is only black tea, not green tea. In addition, the entire territory of Morocco is inhabited by Muslims who only use green tea and do not use black tea. He does not believe that heavy taxes will be imposed. The only place where tea tax may be imposed is Algiers, but he is not sure whether the area is currently imposing taxes.

The Procedure for Ping City Council to Purchase Silver is Negotiated, and the First Batch of 10 Million Yuan Will Be Shipped to Shanghai Soon 140

The Xinxin News Agency reported that the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee, entrusted by the Ministry of Finance, purchased 20 million yuan of silver from Hong Kong. This matter has been confirmed by the banking community. The first batch of silver, about 10 million yuan, will be shipped to Shanghai at the end of the week or the beginning of next week. The remaining will be shipped in succession. The Xinxin News Agency reporter inquired about the details from all parties yesterday, and they are recorded as follows:

Motivation for Purchasing Silver 141

Shanghai's silver reserves have been affected by U.S. silver purchases and China's foreign trade deficit. Last year, the silver outflowed amounted to as much as 200 million yuan. After the central government increased the silver export tax, the outflow gradually decreased. Recently, as the Lunar New Year is approaching in Shanghai, most of the money houses and shops are settling accounts at this time, and cash is needed at that time. The Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications were entrusted by the Ministry of Finance to coordinate the Lunar New Year issue. After several discussions among the three banks, it was decided to purchase 20 million yuan of silver from Hong Kong and ship it to Shanghai to cope with it. The Central Bank is responsible for all the formalities to be handled. This is the general situation of the motivation and process of purchasing silver.

Purchasing Methods 142

There have been various rumors about the method of purchasing silver and importing it, and there is no consensus. Some say that part of the 20 million yuan is to retrieve the silver previously deposited abroad, and some say that it is temporarily borrowed from foreign banks with considerable interest. Others say that it is exchanged for gold bars, and it is said that more than 28,800 gold bars have been shipped out in exchange in recent days. The Xinxin News Agency reporter inquired about the details from Xi Demao, a member of the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee. Xi declined to express any opinion on this matter, only saying that the purchase of silver was entrusted by the Ministry of Finance and would soon be seen in reality. Therefore, the content of the purchase method is currently unable to be confirmed.

Shipped to Shanghai This Week 143

Since the Central Bank began handling all the formalities for shipping silver, they have been completely negotiated. As for the method of shipping silver, due to the excessive amount, it was decided to transport it in batches. The first batch of about 10 million yuan will be shipped to Shanghai at the end of this week or the beginning of next week, and the remaining amount will also be shipped to Shanghai in succession. Therefore, the financial market in this city will be more stable as a result.

Pirates from Dapeng Bay Secretly Come to Shanghai, and the Hai Zhen Ship Was Strictly Inspected Yesterday Before Exporting 147

There were ten pirates in total, and their whereabouts were very secret. The various shipping companies in Shanghai must quickly prepare for emergencies. The various shipping companies, after receiving this warning, immediately issued an emergency alert order to prevent accidents.

Maiden Voyage of the Hai Zhen 148

The Bureau, after receiving the above warning, immediately informed the captain in secret for the safety of the passengers, and notified the maritime police to carry out the inspection before the ship set sail. Measures for Anti-Theft on Ships Total Six Items 150

Since the New Hai Men Ship was stolen, the Administrative Inspector of the Third Special District of Zhejiang Province and the Shanghai Shipping Association have discussed the implementation of anti-theft measures, and a total of six items have been decided. The first item is that the radio equipment on all sea vessels must be fully installed before March. It was resolved that all vessels should be installed accordingly. The second item is that all sea vessels should be equipped with emergency mechanisms, all of which must be installed before the end of February. The emergency mechanisms are to be managed by the shipowner. The third item is how to organize the inspection station. It was resolved that the local land and naval military police and the Shipping Bureau should jointly form an inspection station. The fourth item is that armed maritime police should be added to each vessel, and weapons should be borrowed from the maritime police. The fifth item is the inspection of the distress signal equipment on each vessel, which is to be inspected by the Shipping Administration Bureau. The sixth item is the cost of improving the equipment, which is intended to be offset by increasing the price of cargo and passenger tickets. The above six anti-theft measures will be implemented on the Wenzhou, Taizhou, Haimen, Shipu, Chuanshan, and other regular ships.

Extension of the Deadline for Clearing Old Land Tax Debts by Half a Month 151

The Finance Bureau of this city previously stated that the amount of land tax owed in various districts over the years was very large, and formulated a clearing plan, which was submitted to the Municipal Government for approval, and the clearing period was from December 16 of last year to the end of the month. It ordered the land tax collection offices to follow the plan and summon the local Bao to clear the old debts on schedule, and then set a date for urging collection. Now that the deadline has passed, in addition to the part that has been cleared, the rest have not been cleared on schedule because there are many Bao in various places who are colluding, and it takes time to sort them out. It is heard that the Finance Bureau has submitted a request to the Municipal Government for approval to extend the deadline from January 4 of this year, so that it can continue to handle it. During this extension period, the Bao in various places must bring their grain debt tickets and the grain payments received to the land tax collection office under their jurisdiction for accurate verification and accounting. If they fail to report and conceal the facts, they will be detained and investigated.

Resolution of Commission Dispute for Rice Sales 152

The rice industry in this city has always stipulated that the commission for merchants selling rice in Shanghai is 20 cents per dan. Previously, the rice industry requested an increase in the commission from 20 cents to 25 cents, and some even advocated increasing it to 30 cents. As a result, the general merchants rose up in opposition. On the 7th of this month, the merchants announced a market shutdown. Later, Jiang Shizhi of the Rice Sales Industry Association and Jiang Zisheng of the Rice Industry Association took the initiative to mediate and persuaded the merchants to resume business first. After both parties agreed on a compromise, it was decided that from the 7th, the commission was set at 25 cents per dan, and Jiang Shizhi and others would pay a security deposit. If there was any sabotage, it would be deducted from the security deposit. Those who discovered and reported secret sabotage would be given a bonus to ensure compliance by both parties. It is learned that the plan has been agreed upon by both parties and will be implemented immediately.

Mingxing Ship Changes Date of Sailing to Ningbo, Industry Opposes Strongly, Shipping Administration Bureau Has Been Asked to Handle 154

The Sanbei Mingxing Ship has now changed its sailing date to the 14th. When it was preparing to open the Shanghai-Ningbo route, the company asked the three companies on the same route, China Merchants, Taikoo, and Ning Shao, to reorganize and cooperate and re-determine the apportionment ratio. Traditionally, the Shanghai-Ningbo route was divided into 42.5 shares, with Sanbei accounting for 10 shares, China Merchants accounting for 10.05 shares, and Taikoo and Ning Shao each accounting for 11 shares. This time, Mingxing joined. According to Sanbei's request, the four companies still shared the shares, but Sanbei had two ships, and the total was changed to 46 shares. Taikoo, China Merchants, and Ning Shao each got 10 shares, and Sanbei got 16 shares. At the time, under public discussion, it was believed that Sanbei had been receiving subsidies from the three companies every year. Normally, the Ningxing ship could not match the business of any of the other three ships. Now, if it wanted to add another ship and get more shares, the losses of each company would be even greater, so they unanimously opposed it. At that time, the Shipping Administration Bureau intervened to mediate, but to no avail.

Ship Runs Between Shanghai and Ningbo Should Be Reduced 155

According to various companies, business on the Shanghai-Ningbo route last year was not good. With the cooperation of four ships, they could barely cover expenses. When the Dah Sing's Hong Sing Wheel added to the route, the four companies simultaneously stated that it was actually difficult to add more ships to the Shanghai-Ningbo route. Now, with five ships sailing, according to the statistics of each company, each of the five ships travels back and forth 155 times annually, with some traveling 153 times. The total annual round trip capacity of the five ships is 8.8 million tons. However, the total cargo loaded last year was only 143,872 tons. On average, less than two tons of cargo is loaded per hundred tons of capacity. From the perspective of the main business of transportation, the Shanghai-Ningbo route has a large amount of unused tonnage, which is not in line with the principles of production. The most powerful proof that there is only a need to reduce ships and no need to add routes is that.

Submission to the Navigation Bureau for Handling 156

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Ning Shao Company, etc., yesterday, based on the above statistics, stated that the shipping industry is sluggish, and there is no need to add ships to the Shanghai-Ningbo route in reality. With the current five ships, there is still a sense that there are too many ships and too little cargo, resulting in excessive tonnage. Once Ming Xing joins this line again, it will add another 155 trips per year, with each trip estimated at 5,000 tons, requiring an additional 700,000 tons of capacity. However, the volume of cargo going back and forth is decreasing rather than increasing, which will inevitably lead to a wave of competition. Therefore, they have jointly submitted a request to the Maritime Administration Bureau, requesting a fair and equitable handling of the issue of adding routes to the Shanghai-Ningbo line.

The Covenant is About to Fall Apart 157

According to people from various shipping companies on the same route, if the Sanbei Ming Xing Wheel does not operate on the Ningbo route, the covenant of the four companies can still be continued by finding a way. Now, the Ming Xing Wheel seems to have been scheduled to sail to Ningbo on the 14th. If this wheel operates on the Shanghai-Ningbo line, the cooperation and unity covenant of the four companies will be torn to shreds, and the future of business is not optimistic.

The Central Bank Establishes a Miscellaneous Silver Material Collection and Exchange Office, Supervised by the Business Bureau, Preparations Have Been Completed 159

Since the implementation of the abolition of taels and the conversion to yuan, the silver furnace industry and the public appraisal bureau have been ordered to suspend operations. The Shanghai Silver Industry Association, in view of the problem of exchanging miscellaneous silver in the interior, submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance for approval. The Ministry approved the import and at the same time ordered the Central Bank to establish a miscellaneous silver material collection and exchange office. If merchants hold this miscellaneous silver, they can request the Central Bank to collect and exchange it in accordance with Article 11 of the Silver Standard Coinage Regulations.

Preparations Completed 160

After receiving the order, the Central Bank immediately handed it over to Xi Demao, the manager of the Business Bureau, for preparing the establishment. Now the preparations have been completed, and it is decided to establish it before the end of this month. The bank has submitted a reply to the Ministry of Finance, which will be ordered by the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Silver and Money Industry Association to comply with. The address of the collection and exchange office is attached to the Central Bank, and the exchange rules have been announced.

Regulations Stipulated 161

The exchange rules stipulate that miscellaneous silver materials weighing more than 1,500 grams are not applicable. When miscellaneous silver materials are handed over to the bank for collection and exchange, a positive and negative application form must be filled out. The weight of miscellaneous silver materials is generally based on the standard system. After the bank estimates the fineness and weight, it will be calculated in accordance with the provisions of the Silver Standard Coinage Regulations, with each yuan converted into 23.493448 grams of pure silver, and the minting fee and smelting fee will be deducted according to law. For places outside of Shanghai, the bank's exchange fee should also be added. The bank has the right to refuse to collect and exchange miscellaneous silver materials when there is a question. Miscellaneous silver materials that have already been exchanged cannot be applied for recovery or objection afterward.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Explains the Regulations for Affixing Stamps to Invoices 169

The Current Provisional Regulations on Stamp Tax

Regardless of the Amount, Affix a Stamp Worth One Fen

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce received a letter from the Redwood and Board Industry Association, requesting an explanation of the number of stamps required for invoices, with the price ranging from one yuan to one thousand yuan. The association's reply is now recorded as follows: "The payment receipts or reconciliation statements, which are the invoices you mentioned in your letter, can be exempt from affixing stamps in accordance with Article 3, Section 9 of the new Stamp Tax Law. However, because the law has been promulgated but has not yet stipulated the date of implementation in accordance with Article 24, the current provisional regulations on stamp tax still apply. In accordance with the supplementary measures of the Ministry of Finance, these year-end invoices with the nature of payment reminders, regardless of the amount, must be affixed with a stamp worth one fen. Please check and forward this to your colleagues for compliance."

According to Shen Shi News Agency, the import tax on soybean oil was increased from 15% to 30% since November 20 last year, as announced by Jianghai Customs, and was originally intended to be levied at the same tax rate as food. It has been submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval. Therefore, more than a dozen ships of oil merchants in this port who shipped from various ports in the Northeast before the tax increase all paid taxes according to the new tax regulations. The merchants were unable to bear the burden and repeatedly sent representatives to Beijing to petition for the withdrawal of the order. On the one hand, the Customs Administration ordered oil merchants to temporarily pay the increased tax under seal in order to alleviate the difficulties of the merchants. Yesterday, the reporter of Shen Shi News Agency learned that the authorities of the Ministry of Finance believed that soybean oil is a necessary food for the general public. The Jianghai Customs' proposed method of increasing the tax by analogy with food was ordered to be disapproved. It has been ordered by Jianghai Customs to notify merchants to continue to levy the old tax of 15%, and all taxes paid under seal will be returned.

The Lujiang Disaster Report Received by the Drought Relief Association 175

The Joint Relief Association for Drought Disasters in Various Provinces recently received a report from Fang Jun Songru, the Director-General of Urgent Relief Inspection in Lujiang County, stating that Lujiang suffered a major drought this year. The county has few dikes and many mountains, and the people are poor and the land is barren. After the previous flood, the vitality has not recovered. In addition, the price of grain is low, hurting farmers, and the banditry is constantly disturbing the bankruptcy and borrowing. Those who lend are unable to take care of themselves. Hunger is waiting for death, and moaning is unbearable. There is no rain in summer and autumn, and there are many refugees in winter. There are many dead on the road in spring. It is even worse than the disaster in the sixth year of Xianfeng. The south area of Mian Township totals 318 forts. At this time, the inspection has passed halfway. The disaster is heavy, and the tickets are few. It is really less than one in a hundred living. The winter relief is very difficult, and the crowd of those who have not received relief are stretching their necks and enduring hunger. Those who are shivering from the cold are everywhere. Saving one more life is better than building a seven-level pagoda. Please allocate funds for distribution. The association has checked the severity of the drought in Anhui Province, which is more than ordinary. The disaster situation in Lujiang County is like this, and other places can be known. The public officials and elders of the homeland in Anhui, in the heart of compassion, send out the thoughts of compassion, push food to release clothes, and there are many people. It is hoped that people will be brought back to life, and bones will be made white. Even in the midst of severe winter hunger, seeing righteousness and acting bravely will bring immeasurable blessings. This is what is hoped from the great philanthropists who save their hometown and neighbors.

Yonggu Paint Company Invents Spray Paint to Prevent Leakage, Most Suitable for Painting Ships and Automobiles 179

Although paint is a special product of our country, in recent years, science has advanced rapidly, and European and American countries have manufactured various artificial paints, such as spray paint, which is used for new-era buildings, automobiles, ships, and steel appliances, with beautiful luster. My country's scientific evolution is immature, and there is no such product at the beginning. Therefore, those used in the market are purchased from Europe and the United States, and the leakage is very large. Chen Ciping, the manager of Yonggu Paint Company on Jiangwan Road in this city, in order to recover the rights and interests, has been researching for several years. Recently, according to scientific principles, he invented a kind of spray paint, which is comparable to imported products and even surpasses them. It is suitable for new-style buildings and painting ships and automobiles. Economical and durable, it is indeed a rare high-quality spray paint in domestic paint.

Hu Yizang Compiles a General Treatise on Japanese Zaibatsu 184

The entire book is 150,000 words long.

Including large, medium, and small Zaibatsu

The structure of Japanese Zaibatsu is unprecedented in the world, and the relationship between Zaibatsu and military warlords and political parties is particularly special. Mr. Hu Yizang has translated and compiled "A General Treatise on Japanese Zaibatsu" with reference to "A Theory of Japanese Zaibatsu" by Suzuki Mosaburo and "A Theory of Zaibatsu" by Baiyun Sanren, and added detailed annotations at the end of each chapter. He dissects and analyzes Japanese large, medium, and small Zaibatsu, as well as local Zaibatsu, one by one. The content is quite detailed, such as the Mitsui, Mitsubishi, and Sumitomo among the large Zaibatsu, the Kuhara, Mori, Noguchi, and Nakajima families among the emerging Zaibatsu, the Yasuda, Kawasaki, Shibuzawa, and Yamaguchi families among the banking capital, the Asano, Okura, Nezu, Okawa, Tanaka, Furukawa, Fujita, and Kawanishi families among the industrial capital, the Yamashita, Okazaki, and Iwamoto families centered on shipping, as well as the cartels, trusts, conglomerates, and unions of the Zaibatsu. He has collected everything exhaustively. Mr. Hu took Suzuki Mosaburo's "Theory of Japanese Zaibatsu" as a blueprint, and then referred to and translated Baiyun Sanren's "Theory of Zaibatsu," carefully studying and revising it with great effort. The entire book is about 150,000 words long and will be printed soon. For those who want to understand the Japanese political and economic situation, the Zaibatsu's control over politics, the relationship between them, and the investment status between the Zaibatsu, there is no other great work in the country besides this book.

The Ta Mei Evening News reports that on January 2nd, a fire broke out accidentally in the servants' room of a foreign house at 361 Anhe Temple Road, and morphine manufacturing equipment and a large number of raw materials were found in the main house. The owner of the house, an Englishman named Xiang Sheng, has recently returned to his country. His wife was arrested two days later and released on bail of 2,000 yuan. A Large Number of Raw Materials 189

In addition, there were countless porcelain funnels of various sizes, a huge furnace, and various packages and chemical bottles. The defendant was charged with violating the British government's 1924 ban on narcotics in China by manufacturing narcotics. This morning, she sat silently behind her lawyer with a sullen face. First, the prosecutor, Li Kesi, stated that the defendant not only violated national laws but also greatly opposed humanitarianism. The British government had recently assisted the Chinese government in Geneva in eliminating the huge harm of the narcotics trade, and the Chinese government had issued a clear order that anyone who trafficked drugs would be sentenced to death, and even those who smoked drugs would also be subject to this severe penalty. Last year, in this area, there were

Executions by Firing Squad 190

There were as many as 114 people who violated narcotics laws. There is credible evidence that the defendant was engaged in the narcotics trade. This behavior of the defendant is a reckless abuse of the favorable treatment enjoyed by foreigners in China and insults the reputation of the British Emperor. Li Kesi then described in detail the circumstances of the case and said that the defendant had refused to open the door that day to allow the detectives to inspect, claiming that she had no keys. Later, a locksmith was called to open the door, and the morphine manufacturing equipment was discovered. The defendant then fainted and fell to the ground. The defendant's husband went to Europe in December of last year. Is of Particular Importance 191

When asked what the three words meant, she replied that she was telling her husband that she and the baby were safe. A Western Police Chief Commits Suicide as a Result of a Love Triangle The Police Station Investigates the Truth 195

Kinnas Lyon, a Western police chief at the Jing'an Temple Police Station in the Public Concession, is a British national, 32 years old, and is amiable and approachable. He has never spoken harshly or sternly, so all Chinese and Western police officers in the police station are happy to befriend him. Lyon has not yet married, but it is said that he had a love affair with a Chinese woman, but soon Lyon cohabited with a Russian girl, and the Russian girl is already pregnant and about to give birth. Unexpectedly, the affair was discovered by the Chinese woman, who was burning with jealousy and immediately launched a major interrogation. In this situation, Lyon felt embarrassed and looked troubled. He was a completely different person from before. On the morning of the 7th, Lyon suddenly claimed to be ill and asked the police station for leave. At that time, the matter was considered normal, so no one suspected anything else. However, at about 1:00 p.m. the day before yesterday (the 8th), Lyon suddenly shot himself in the head with a double-barreled shotgun in the police station dormitory. By the time the police station staff arrived after hearing the sound, Lyon was already lying stiff in a pool of blood, dead. Tenant Extorts Landlord Case Cui Ziguang Sentenced to One Year and Six Months in Prison 199

Cui Ziguang, a 25-year-old man from Suzhou, lives in the pavilion room on the upper floor of the Jingmei Cake Shop (owned by 47-year-old Ningbo native Wu Xingkang) at No. 141 Avenue Joffre in the French Concession. He used to be in the bread business, but has recently been unemployed and idle. He is struggling financially and lives with his elderly mother, wife, and children. He saw that the second landlord, Wu Xingkang, the owner of the cake shop, was making a profit from his business and had a small amount of savings, so he had bad intentions. On November 27, November 29, December 7, December 19, and December 20 of last year, Cui, under the name of Zheng Jinbiao, wrote five threatening letters in a row and sent them to Wu Xingkang through the post office, demanding 5,000 yuan. The first four letters asked to contact him at the Mass Education Cooperative in Wenmiao Park. The fifth letter changed the location to the Deyitea House in Yuyuan Garden in Yemiao. On the one hand, he volunteered to Wu and was willing to be a representative to contact the bandits. On December 20, Cui replied to Wu that the bandits had agreed to reduce the amount, but needed 500 yuan. Wu, unable to pay, asked Cui to discuss reducing the amount of money again. The next day, Cui falsely told Wu that after exhausting all discussions, at least 150 yuan was needed, otherwise it would not be possible to settle the matter. Wu, in order to settle the matter, gave Cui 70 yuan on the evening of the 21st and asked him to pay it first, and the remaining 80 yuan would be paid when he had raised the money. Unexpectedly, the matter was discovered by Inspector Jin Jiulin of the French Concession Police, who sent detectives Zhou Buguang and Cai Jinzhang and patrolman Zhu Jutong to wait in ambush at the Jingmei Cake Shop on the 22nd. Before long, they saw Cui go out and followed him, intending to secretly arrest the extortionist bandits. Who knew that Cui was carrying the 70 yuan given by Wu Xingkang and went out to buy a wallet at a department store first, and then set off for the Chinese community. The detectives followed behind and saw that Cui did not take the Yemiao route, but walked towards Tongqing Street. The detectives followed him to the end of Tongqing Street and, thinking that Cui was suspicious, they rushed up to stop and question him. Cui confessed that he had written threatening letters in order to defraud money for his own use. The detectives then arrested Cui, took him to the Public Security Bureau for filing, and then took him back to the French Concession Police Station to obtain the five threatening letters from Wu Xingkang and sent him to the Second Special District Court. The police lawyer filed a public prosecution against Cui for the crimes of extortion and fraud. The details of the interrogation have been recorded in previous newspapers. The case has been investigated by Judge Zhang Chaozuo, who yesterday opened the court and briefly interrogated Cui and sentenced Cui Ziguang to one year and six months of imprisonment for fraud. The number of days detained before the judgment was determined to be two days for one day of imprisonment. The five letters were confiscated and the stolen money was returned to the victim. After the sentence, the defendant was taken into custody at the detention center, awaiting the expiration of the appeal period before being sent to prison for execution.

A Young Woman Died Tragically from a Quarrel Between Husband and Wife A Miscarriage Caused by Beating and a Big Disturbance at the Morgue 200

Wu Zhigang (i.e., Shuchun), a deceased local man who lived at No. 2 Wu Family Residence, South End, Longhua Town, used to sell drugs and made a lot of profit, so his family had a lot of savings. His wife, Cai, gave birth to four sons and two daughters. The second son, Jiagen, is now 22 years old and works as a teacher in a private school. Two years ago, he married Lu Linyun, a 21-year-old local woman from Xinqiaotou who works as a cook, through a matchmaker. After entering the house, they were initially harmonious, but recently they have often quarreled, and Jiagen has a very fierce temper and often beats her severely. On October 18th of last year, Lu was injured by being beaten and filed a complaint with the police station, but it was later withdrawn after persuasion from relatives. Unexpectedly, the night before last, Jiagen beat and kicked Lu again for the second time, causing her to be bruised all over and her body to be covered in injuries. This triggered a miscarriage (Lu was six months pregnant), and she died the next morning. When Lu's parents and relatives found out about this, they rushed to see her and saw the deceased lying on a board, her whole body purple and her blood stained all over the place. Wu's entire family, men and women, had already fled, leaving only Wang Xiaoshanzi, a Yancheng native hired temporarily, to watch over the body. They took Wang Xiaoshanzi to the Longhua Security Group and temporarily detained him, and burned all of Lu's dowry. Later, Cai Rongxiang, the head of the district, came out to mediate and agreed to handle the funeral generously. However, it is still being persuaded whether the Lu family will comply.

The Case of the Chief of the Haimen Public Security Sub-Bureau Being Accused of Massacreing Innocents is Concluded in Shanghai 202

Prosecuted for Murder After a Clear Investigation by the Prosecutor

The Details of the Case were Clarified Yesterday and the Sentence is Scheduled for the 14th

Hong Weiqing, a Haimen native, accused Miao Fengxiang, the patrolman of the Second Sub-Bureau of the Haimen Changle Town Public Security Bureau, and Jing, the chief of the Seventh Sub-Bureau of the Haimen Public Security Bureau, of premeditated murder in the Shanghai Local Court. His statement roughly stated that his younger brother, Hong Weixin, was tragically killed by the defendants on December 24th, 1919, after being framed. He appealed according to the law, requesting redress. However, the defendants colluded with new and old local bullies and added evil forces day by day, threatening and intimidating him, making it difficult to fulfill his wish. Fortunately, the fellow villagers in Shanghai deeply knew of Weixin's grievance, so they organized a support association. It has been more than three years since it was sent to your court for investigation. The defendants rely on having a lot of money,

Vast Divine Powers 203

Not only did he evade appearing in court, but he also openly declared that a certain matter had been arranged, and a certain issue was no longer a problem, saying that if the accuser appeared in court, he would be dealt with in the same manner as the deceased. As a result, the accuser had no way to redress the injustice. Subsequently, after the Shanghai-Qidong Victims' Support Association sent personnel to inquire about the reasons why the accusers did not appear in court, it was learned that they had received a summons from your esteemed court. The first defendant, Miao Fengxiang, had been taken into custody and requested to be brought to justice. The presiding judge in this case, Prosecutor Yang An, repeatedly held court hearings, conducted thorough interrogations, and prosecuted the case in accordance with the law, charging the accused with murder and requesting a public trial for Jing Bi, Miao Fengxiang, and others.

Criminal Facts 204

Jing Bi, as the Director of the 7th Branch of the Public Security Bureau of Haimen County, was by nature rude and brutal, and extremely fond of killing. On November 4th of the 19th year of the Republic, taking advantage of the rampant communist bandits in Haimen County, he used the pretext of suppressing bandits and shot and killed a teahouse customer named Yang Zhaoti in the Shiyun Road teahouse in Dacheng Town. Afterwards, he falsely reported that Yang Zhaoti was a bandit who opened fire to resist arrest and was killed on the spot. On December 24th of the same year, in front of the Shi family residence about three li south of Sanxing Town, he ordered Patrol Officer Miao Fengxiang to shoot and kill a suspected bandit named Hong Weixin, also falsely reporting that Hong Weixin had seized a gun to resist arrest and was killed on the spot. The Shanghai-Qidong Victims' Support Association filed a complaint with the Control Yuan.

Transfer for Disciplinary Action 205

The Central Public Servants Disciplinary Committee sent a letter to the Jiangsu Higher Court, transferring the case for investigation. (Reasons for prosecution and legal provisions violated) In this case, Jing Bi, Miao Fengxiang, and others, using the pretext that Yang Zhaoti and Hong Weixin were bandits, arbitrarily and indiscriminately killed them on the grounds of opening fire to resist arrest. The family members of the victims, Huang Dingyi, Hong Liu Shi, Hong Weiqing, and others, appeared in court to provide detailed accounts. Furthermore, Mao Xian, an investigator from the Control Yuan, went to the scene of the crime to investigate and confirmed the facts. Upon reviewing the original county files, it was found that Jing Bi's report stated that Yang Zhaoti and several accomplices were conspiring in the Shiyun Road teahouse. When the officers attempted to arrest them, Yang Zhaoti and one of his accomplices each

Drew Firearms 206

And resisted the officers. Seeing that the bandits continued to fire and were extremely fierce, fearing danger, the officers fired back, hitting Yang Zhaoti in the chest, causing him to fall and die immediately. This account does not match the original county coroner's report, which stated that Yang Zhaoti had three bullet wounds in his back, with entry wounds on the spine and exit wounds on the chest. Moreover, according to the teahouse owner Shi Yunlu's testimony in the original county court, "I only heard three gunshots that day. When I went into the room, Yang Zhaoti had already been shot dead." This indicates that Yang Zhaoti did not open fire to resist arrest at the time, making it clear that Jing Bi arbitrarily and indiscriminately killed him without a doubt. As for Hong Weixin,

Regarding the Murder 207

Although Miao Fengxiang argued, "After Director Jing and I apprehended Hong Weixin, while passing about three li south of Sanxing Town, Hong Weixin seized the gun of police officer Lu Shunkang and attempted to escape, and opened fire to resist arrest. Director Jing then ordered us to fire back, and the bullets entered from the back," this account does not match the original county coroner's report, which stated that Hong Weixin had one bullet wound on his right forehead, with the bullet exiting from the back of his head, and one bullet wound in his chest, with the bullet exiting from his spine. Moreover, it was testified, "There were five or six police officers with us at the time, and each of us carried firearms. If Hong Weixin had indeed

Seized a Gun to Resist 208

Why were none of Jing Bi and the other five or six officers injured? Furthermore, since he had already been arrested, how could he have had the opportunity to seize a firearm, and how would he have dared to use a seized gun to resist five or six firearms? His defense is clearly an attempt to evade responsibility. Considering their actions, Jing Bi committed two offenses under Article 43 of the Criminal Code and Article 282, Paragraph 1 of the same law. Miao Fengxiang committed one offense under Article 282, Paragraph 1 of the same law. Both should be punished in accordance with Article 2 of the Amnesty Law and Article 140 of the Criminal Code. Therefore, they are prosecuted under Article 253 of the Criminal Procedure Law. The case was heard by Judge Guan Liting, but no conclusion was reached. Yesterday morning, Judge Guan specially opened the

For the trial. About three or four years ago, I went to visit my sick nephew and saw five or six policemen escorting Hong Weixin eastward. I was walking westward. Because I was afraid, I walked along the riverbank. And shooting him to death. The judge asked, "Do you recognize Miao Fengxiang?" He replied, "I do." The judge ordered Miao Fengxiang, who was in custody, to be brought to the stand.
