[The Shanghai South Shelter for the Poor is Overcrowded] 212

Two Shelters Have Reached Over Two Thousand People

Women, Children, and the Poor are Temporarily Not Being Accepted

The Shanghai South Shelter for the Poor has been receiving a large number of poor people recently. The shelter submitted a document to the United Charities Association yesterday, stating, "Respectfully submitting this report, as of the 5th of this month, excluding those sent to drug rehabilitation centers and hospitals for treatment, both shelters house a total of 1,940 poor people. The second shelter, located in the Chao Hui Villa, opened on the 1st of this month. The number of poor people seeking shelter has been increasing continuously. The total number of new and old cotton clothes and pants is less than 1,000 sets, which is not enough to distribute completely to the poor people. We are deeply concerned about this insufficiency. The daily requirement for rice is currently over 15 shi. It is estimated that the number of people seeking shelter this year will be even greater than in previous years. We hereby respectfully request your esteemed association to expand fundraising, especially for cotton clothes and pants, to avoid difficulties in providing for the needs of the shelter. We are submitting a report on the income and expenses of the shelter from December 1st to December 31st of last year for your review. This is for your convenience." At the same time, the shelter sent a document to the Public Security Bureau, stating, "Respectfully replying to your letter regarding the establishment of a second shelter and requesting that stray poor people be sent for shelter. We have instructed our subordinates to comply. After investigating, the total number of poor people sheltered in both shelters has reached over 2,000. Although the weather is not yet very cold, the number of people seeking shelter has been increasing continuously. However, due to the difficulties in managing and providing for women and children, we do not yet have facilities for women, making it difficult to accommodate them. We are hereby respectfully requesting that you take this into consideration and instruct your subordinate branches and teams to send only male stray poor people to our shelter. Please make other arrangements for female and child stray poor people to avoid causing inconvenience. We are grateful for your consideration."

Two Railways Change the Procedures for Using Free Ride Passes 213

The Two Railways Administration issued an order to all departments, stating, "Upon investigation, Article 8 of the Provisional Regulations for Employees and Their Families to Use Official Business Ride Passes or Free Ride Passes, promulgated by this administration, stipulates that a Family Ride Pass Form should be attached when issuing Free Ride Passes to employees' families. The original intention of this law was to facilitate ticket inspectors to check whether the age of the user matches the information recorded on the pass, thereby preventing abuses. When employees themselves use the pass, their badge and service certificate can be checked, making it unnecessary to attach a pass form. However, some departments have also attached this pass form when issuing Free Ride Passes to employees themselves, which is unnecessarily repetitive and cumbersome. It is hereby stipulated that from January 1, 1935, Family Ride Pass Forms will no longer be attached when employees themselves apply for Free Ride Passes. A stamp stating 'Badge and Service Certificate Required for Ticket Inspection on the Train' will be added to the pass. The procedures for employees' families to apply for Free Ride Passes will remain the same. To simplify the procedures, receipts for employees and their families applying for Free Ride Passes will be cancelled from January 1st of this year. This order is hereby issued for compliance."

Municipal Industrial Testing Institute Adds Industrial Guidance 214

The Municipal Industrial Testing Institute on Xiafei Road, established by the Municipal Government to support the development of industry and commerce and guide the improvement of their products, has achieved remarkable results since its opening. The number of commissioned tests, research projects, and certifications has been increasing daily, benefiting all sectors of industry and commerce. It has recently been learned that, in view of the increasing number of requests for the institute to dispatch personnel to provide on-site guidance and for technical problems to be studied at the institute, in order to meet the needs of society, the institute has added an Industrial Guidance section. The scope of guidance will initially cover two areas: chemical industry and textile industry. All regulations have been submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and implementation.

Committing Murder Due to a Mistress's Infidelity, then Committing Suicide Out of Fear of Punishment 215

Yin Zhuqing Severely Stabs His Mistress

Escapes and Dies by Poisoning in a Hotel

Yin Zhuqing, a 56-year-old man from Taixing, lived at No. 6, Huiyuan Lane, Huade Road. He was previously a driver at the tram company and is now unemployed. A year ago, he became acquainted with Zhang Yumei, a 30-year-old woman from Liyang, and rented a room on the front floor of No. 14, Songjia Lane, Beijing Road, as a place for their rendezvous. Initially, the two were quite loving, but in the past month, the woman, seeing that Yin's money was running out and that he was old, became romantically involved with a man surnamed Tan. This was suddenly discovered, so on the afternoon of the day before yesterday, at about 5:00 PM, he secretly hid a razor and went to Zhang's place, falsely claiming that someone from his hometown had come to Shanghai and invited Zhang and her niece, Song Shupan (age 13), to visit together. They took the No. 7 tram to Tilanqiao, then walked to a remote area on Beiqiwupu Road, Pei Kai'er Road. Yin suddenly grabbed Zhang Yumei by the hair and strangled her neck. (At this time, the girl Song was frightened and ran home.) He then stabbed Zhang six times in the face and other areas with the razor. Zhang cried out for help, and they dispersed. Yin, fearing punishment, went to Room 34 of the Continental Hotel, No. 640, Lane 6, Huade Road, and committed suicide by poisoning himself. Zhang went to the Yulin Road Police Station to report what happened. The police station ordered Deputy Inspector Yang Peisheng and detectives Pan Yunlong to investigate. A razor with bloodstains, a wooden comb, and some hair were found at the scene. They went to Yin's house, but he was not there. They went to nearby hotels to investigate. At about 5:00 AM the next morning, they found Yin in the Continental Hotel, but he was groaning in bed from poisoning. They took him to the Sacred Heart Hospital, but he died despite treatment. The body was taken to the Forensic Examination Office on Feilun Road. Zhang is also being treated in the hospital, and her injuries are quite serious. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special District District Court, accompanied by forensic doctors Wei and Zhang and clerk Wang Zuyi, went to the office to examine the body. First, the detectives reported the results of their investigation. Then, Song Shuji, a 13-year-old girl, testified, "Zhang Yumei is my aunt. We live together at No. 14, Songjia Lane, Beijing Road. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday, at about 5:00 PM, Yin suddenly came and invited Zhang and me to visit relatives in Tilanqiao. Later, at Qiwupu Road, Yin suddenly grabbed my aunt's hair and strangled her neck. I was terrified and ran home." Yin Genfu testified, "I am a coppersmith at the tram company. The deceased is my father. I don't know how he died. He has spent two or three thousand yuan on Zhang. I request justice." After Guo Jun obtained the testimony, he ordered that the deceased Yin Zhuqing, a male, had indeed died by poisoning himself before his death. The body was handed over to his son Yin Genfu for burial. It was also learned that Zhang Yumei was a prostitute.

Electrical Fire at Qianfeng Rubber Shoe Factory on Qingyun Road, Zhabei 221

Burning Shen Peixing

Losses Estimated at Tens of Thousands

The Qianfeng Rubber Shoe Factory at No. 87, Shishou Lane, next to the World Grand Theater on Qingyun Road, Zhabei, was founded by He Tiehua, a comprador of the China Merchants Bureau's Northern Wharf. It has been in operation for a long time and is a large-scale factory with as many as nine buildings. At about 10:30 PM last night, an electrical fire broke out on the upper floor of the factory. Because it was next to many barrels of raw rubber, once it caught fire, thick smoke spread and the fire raged. The Zhabei fire brigades rushed to the scene to put out the fire, which was not extinguished until 1:30 AM this morning. Several houses on both sides were also affected. When the fire broke out, the victims were awakened from their sleep and fled with their suitcases and belongings. Their wives cried and their children wailed, gathering by Qingyun Road, which was a heartbreaking scene. Shen Peixing, a 22-year-old coppersmith from Shaoxing, was severely burned and sent to Tongren Hospital by ambulance. It is reported that the losses amounted to tens of thousands.

Book Artist Huang Hongtu Sells His Works in Beijing and Shanghai 225

The great calligrapher Huang Hongtu, styled Xitang, a native of Linchuan, is a respected elder of Jiangxi. He is learned and skilled in writing, particularly excelling in calligraphy. From the inscriptions on bronzes, oracle bones, and turtle shells of the Shang and Zhou dynasties to the rubbings from steles of the Han, Wei, Six Dynasties, Sui, and Tang dynasties, he has meticulously studied and copied them all, developing his unique style. Consequently, those seeking his works come in droves. He is deeply admired by Mr. Chen Shiyi, Mr. Tang Weizhi, Mr. Liu Yimou, Mr. Huang Binhong, Mr. Chen Boxuan, Mr. Chen Zhuzun, Mr. Sun Benwen, Mr. Ouyang Jingwu, and other gentlemen. Currently, at the invitation of friends, he resides in Beijing to sell his calligraphy. Major paper shops in Shanghai also accept orders on his behalf. It is also heard that Mr. Huang, at the request of friends, will open a school in Beijing to teach, passing on the secrets he has uniquely obtained over decades to deserving individuals, which is indeed fortunate for the literary world. The tuition fee is approximately ten yuan per month. He currently resides in Nanjing.

The Four Banks Joint Reserve Depository Issues Its 262nd Reserve Report 226

The Four Banks Joint Reserve Depository is jointly established by the Y盐业, Jin Cheng金城, Zhongnan中南, and Continental大陸 Banks, specializing in issuing banknotes for the Zhongnan Bank. According to the depository's issuing regulations, the issuance of banknotes is fully backed, with at least 60% in cash reserves and up to 40% in guarantee reserves. A public announcement is made weekly, verified by the auditors and accountants of the four banks. Here is a copy of the 262nd announcement of the Shanghai Reserve Depository, dated January 5th, year 24: Banknotes in circulation: 32,070,473 yuan; Total reserves: 32,070,473 yuan, including Cash reserves: 22,469,373 yuan; Guarantee reserves: 9,600,110 yuan.

Attorney Qiu Hanping Relocates His Law Firm 228

Dr. Qiu Hanping, a renowned lawyer in this city, has been practicing law in Shanghai for five years as part of the Minquan Lawyers Group. He is known for his diligence in handling cases and his enthusiasm for various social causes. Due to insufficient office space at his original location at 519 Continental Emporium, he relocated his office on the 7th to the Building at 918 Avenue Edward VII. Attorney Qiu holds a Doctorate of Law from the National University of Kyoto, USA, and is an honorary member of the Roman Law School of the Royal University of Italy. He is well-versed in both Chinese and Western legal theories, as well as ancient and modern legal systems, with a deep understanding of Roman law and comparative law. He has served as the Director of the Department of Diplomacy and Consular Affairs at the National Jinan University, Professor of the University Department of Wusong China Public School, and is currently the new editor of the Law Journal, Professor of the Law School of Soochow University, Professor of Criminal Law at Jinan University, and Director of the Overseas Cultural Affairs Department. Attorney Qiu has authored numerous works, including "International Exchange and Trade" (Minzhi), "Comprehensive Compilation of Law" (Commercial Press), "Pre-Qin Legal Thought" (Wenhua), and "On Chinese Negotiable Instruments Law" (World).

Members of the National Products Preservation Association Take Office Yesterday 229

Yesterday, the 24th Executive and Supervisory Committee of the China National Products Preservation Association held an oath-taking ceremony in the auditorium of the Association's headquarters on Gaodun Street, Nine Acres. Minutes of the Meeting of the Eighth Branch of the Municipal Federation in the Second Special District 230

The Eighth Branch of the Shanghai Municipal Federation of Citizens of the Second Special District, located at the intersection of Avenue Joffre and Rue du Père Froc in the French Concession, convened a temporary emergency meeting yesterday at 4 PM at its headquarters. Nine executive committee members, including Cao Xianda, Zhang Zhiqin, Wu Guowei, and Pan Dafu, were present. After the formal procedures, Chairman Wu Guowei reported that yesterday (i.e., the 8th) at 6:45 PM, after finishing dinner at home and preparing to retire to bed (Wu's residence is located in Shengsheng Li, Qianjiatang South, Huanlong Road, French Concession), suddenly six robbers, two wielding pistols, one with a blackened face, claimed to be searching for red pills and tricked their way into the back door. They went straight upstairs, brandished their guns, and ordered silence. They robbed over two hundred yuan worth of clothing and jewelry, as well as banknotes. Before leaving, they tied everyone in the room before making their escape. Since this case has occurred, residents in the area are now afraid to sleep soundly. He requested that the matter be discussed. The meeting then commenced to discuss the following: (1) Send a letter to the Chief of the General Police Station, requesting the investigation and arrest of the gang of robbers; (2) Request the Chief to order the Zhaozhong Road Police Station to increase the number of patrol officers or plainclothes police in Qianjiatang, closely patrol the area, pay attention to suspicious idlers and vagrants loitering in the area, and take preventive measures to ensure safety; (3) Member Huang Guisheng reported that his father, Xiufeng, was aboard the Jing'an transport ship of the Sanbei Company on December 28th of last year, traveling from Tianjin to Shanghai. En route, the cargo in the ship's hold was piled too high, collapsed, and crushed him to death. The Sanbei Company only agreed to provide a compensation of 200 yuan. He requested assistance in negotiating a settlement to give importance to this death. It was decided to forward a letter to the French Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association and the Municipal Federation of the Second Special District for assistance in upholding justice. Other cases were then discussed, and the meeting adjourned.

City News 231

Chinese-French Products Sell Well in Various Ports of Nanyang The pharmaceuticals produced by the Chinese-French Dispensary have long been sold at home and abroad and are widely popular. Recently, tonic medicines, such as Ai Luo Brain Tonic, Nine-Created Genuine Blood, Red Blood Wheel Tonic, Double Lion Brand Beef Juice, and Baby Chicken Juice, as well as household medicines, such as Ai Luo Lung Medicine, Elephant Brand Apricot Kernel Dew, Luo Wei Pilin Tablets, Ren Dan, Qingsheng Dan, Luo Wei Mai Jing Cod Liver Oil, Chinese-French Headache Sun Cream, Non-Toxic Pain Reliever, Pain Relief Tablets, cosmetics, and Baby Face, have seen a surge in sales in the Nanyang region, with total annual sales exceeding 200,000 yuan in national currency. This demonstrates the enthusiasm of overseas compatriots for using domestic products and the vision and outward-looking efforts of domestic new pharmaceutical businesses, as well as their excellent achievements. The Chinese-French Dispensary is the most prominent example. While the Chinese people know that silk and tea are major items in foreign trade, who would know that there is such news in the new pharmaceutical industry? This is truly good news for the new year. Hua Xing Pharmacy Donates Zeng Wenzhenggong's Diary The Hua Xing Pharmacy in this city has long been famous in society for selling the lung-healing medicine that cures all kinds of coughs. It is now heard that the pharmacy is donating Zeng Wenzhenggong's Diary. A total of 50,000 copies of the diary will be donated until they are all given away. Those who wish to request a copy can enclose two cents in postage (three cents for out-of-town addresses) and send it to China Post Office Box 445. The pharmacy will immediately send the diary.

"Artificial Gold" Rings Sell Well The "artificial gold" rings, newly invented by the French great scientist Mr. Crane Craner, and exclusively managed by the jewelry department of Laison Foreign Firm at 397 Simalu Road in this city, are glittering with gold and of novel design. They have recently arrived in Shanghai. For the sake of popularizing beauty among ladies, the firm is holding a major sacrifice and grand prize event for one month. It is heard that each ring originally costs five yuan, but during the sacrifice period, each ring is sold for only one yuan and two jiao, and two airplane gift certificates are given away. Therefore, customers have been flocking in recent days, and the staff is overwhelmed.

Bovril Beef Juice Sells Well Bovril magical beef juice is a famous British product, with great tonic power and miraculous effect. Last year, on November 13th, 15th, and 16th, the company invited 6,000 doctors and 1,000 female doctors to visit the factory and see the manufacturing process. The factory's equipment prioritizes cleanliness. The cattle used are of excellent breed. During manufacturing, chemists conduct detailed inspections. Therefore, the quality is indeed superior. Major pharmacies in China all sell the product.

All were cured by Dr. Gao. Now that winter has arrived, there is an endless stream of people asking Dr. Gao to prescribe medicinal plasters.

New-Style Movie Theater to Appear in This City Beijing Road in this city is a major east-west thoroughfare in the central district. Since the widening of the section from Zhejiang Road to Xizang Road, the traffic has become even busier. It is heard that someone is building a very magnificent movie theater at the corner of this road and Guizhou Road, naming it the "Capital Grand Theater." The interior has over a thousand seats, all with spring cushions. All the equipment is extremely refined, rivaling the major theaters in this city. Weather Report 236

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated: Shandong and its surrounding areas will have clear and cold weather with winds from southwest to northwest. The middle and lower reaches of the Yangtze River will be overcast and gradually cloudy with some sunny intervals, but there will be fog in the morning, with winds from northwest to north. The East China Sea and the Taiwan Strait will be overcast with fog and gentle northwest to northeast winds. There will be a cyclone and rain around Kyushu, caused by a low pressure moving northeast-east. Furthermore, in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 51.4 and the lowest was 46.3. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 48.2 and the lowest was 40.5.

Educational News

Universal Compulsory Education and Civic Education to Be Implemented from the 24th Year Onward 237

Central Government Orders the Ministry of Education to Comply

(Nanjing, 9th) On the 9th, the National Government issued an order to the Executive Yuan, instructing the Ministry of Education to comply with the resolution of the Fifth Plenary Session of the Fourth Central Committee of the Central Executive Committee, a proposal by 11 committee members including Liu Zhi, regarding the allocation of funds to popularize compulsory education and mass education. The resolution outlines two methods: 1. From the 24th year onward, the central, provincial, and municipal governments must designate funds specifically for compulsory education. 2. If the original education taxes and levies in various counties need to be abolished, compensatory measures must be planned.

Annual Meeting of the Chinese Chemical Industry Association 243

Held in Nanjing for Three Days

The Chinese Chemical Industry Association held its 10th annual meeting in Nanjing from January 4th to 6th, using the library of National Central University as the venue. The situation is briefly recorded below:

Number of Attendees On the morning of the 4th, at 9 o'clock, registered attendees included Shi Ying, Zhao Tingbing, Liao Dingqu, Chen Qi, Dai Ji, Yuan Hanqing, Yu Tongkui, Gong Angyun, Cao Youcheng, Wang Zhaotong, Cheng Yingzhang, Zhong Lieju, Sun Qichang, Cao Liangxia, Jin Peisong, Zhang Kangze, Chen Shizhang, Yang Chengxun, Guan Shizhi, Tao Weisun, Hu Fanruo, Xu Xinzhi, Wu Chengluo, Qian Zhenghua, Fang Xinfang, Zeng Guangfang, Xu Fengshi, Hong Zhong, Zhang Liuyi, Wang Zhaocheng, and Sun Yushou, among others, totaling more than 30 people. A preparatory meeting was held at 10 o'clock. In the evening, a welcome banquet was hosted by Mayor Shi at the Municipal Government.

Theses and Annual Banquet On the morning of the 5th, theses were presented, including Xu Fengshi's "A Preliminary Investigation of Sichuan Salt Wells," Hong Zhong's "An Investigation of Sichuan Natural Gas," Cheng Yanqing and Wang Shicai's "A Quantitative Analysis Method for Mixtures of Potassium Dichromate and Potassium Permanganate," Dai Ji's "Chemical Engineering Research, Chemical Engineering Implementation, and the Smoothness of Finance," Cao Youde's "A New Method for the Quantitative Analysis of Boron in Organic Compounds," Lin Jifang's "A Study of Fennel," and Wang Zhixue's "A Preliminary Study of Volatile Oil in Star Anise Fruit Produced in Guangxi." In the evening, the annual banquet was held at the Central Hotel. Guests included Ding Zaijun, Secretary-General of the Academia Sinica; Gu Yuqun, Director of the Central Industrial Experiment Institute; Chen Yuguang, Director of the National Translation and Compilation Bureau; Chen Kezhong, President of the Chinese Chemical Society; and approximately 30 members. During the banquet, Ding Zaijun, Gu Yuqun, Chen Kezhong, Xu Fengshi, Chen Shizhang, and Yu Tongkui delivered speeches in succession.

General Meeting On the morning of the 6th, the general meeting was held. President Cao Liangxia chaired the meeting, and the procedures were carried out as usual. The chairman reported on the association's activities in the past year, followed by a discussion of proposals. It was resolved: (1) to amend the constitution, the most important of which was to amend the election law and add three election committee members to handle the next election; (2) to cooperate with the Chinese Society of Chemical Engineers to publish publications. At the end was the election. Those elected were: President Cao Liangxia, Vice President Wu YunChu, Secretaries Shao Jialin and Yu Xueyang, Accountant Cheng Yingzhang, General Affairs Guan Shizhi, and Editor Dai Ji. The elected members of the Advisory Committee were Chen Shizhang, He Shangping, and Lin Jiyong. The members of the Election Committee were Chen Shizhang, He Shangping, and Xu Shanxiang. At noon, a welcome banquet was hosted by President Luo Jialun of Central University.

Tours and Visits On the afternoon of the 4th, tours were conducted to Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum, Ming Xiaoling Mausoleum, and Tan's tomb. On the afternoon of the 5th, visits were made to the Academia Sinica Astronomical Observatory, the Central Industrial Experiment Institute, the Central Hygiene Experiment Institute, and Central University.

Gifts to Boost Enthusiasm Shanghai Tianchu MSG Factory, Wuzhou Pharmacy, Family Industry Society, Yonghe Industrial Company, Yifeng Enamel Factory, Da Zhonghua Celluloid Factory, Peacock Chemical Company, Yaguang Bakelite Factory, China Chemical Industry Company, Yabuer Electrical Appliance Company, Commercial Press, Da Hua Industrial Company, Tongyi Refined Salt Company, Zhenhua Paint Factory, Central Chemical Glass Factory, Wenguang Arts and Crafts Company, and Sanyou Industrial Company, and other manufacturers, distributed exquisite products to members and guests to add to the fun.

More than 7,400 Visitors Last Month

The Shanghai Municipal Botanical Garden has been open for several months. Recently, the Municipal Education Bureau sent Shen Xiangrui, the director of the zoo, and Jiang Xiyi, the director of the garden, to the management committee of Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum in Nanjing and the agricultural college of Central University to collect plants. Grading of Examination Papers Begins

The fourth annual graduation examination for middle school students in this city, which began on the 7th of this month and was held at four different venues, was completely finished yesterday. Semester Nearing End, Large Number of Students Going Abroad to Study 247

Most Going to Japan, Followed by England, Germany and Italy, Fewest to France and America

Recently, the number of people seeking assistance from the Shanghai Global Students Association for procedures to study abroad has surged due to the end of the semester. According to Mr. Wu Deyi, from the association’s study abroad reception department, they have already assisted forty to fifty people in processing their applications. Japan is the most popular destination, due to the low value of the yen and the simplicity of the procedures. England and Germany are second. Studying in America and France, which used to account for the majority in the past few years, has become very rare recently. Furthermore, those studying in Italy, who previously constituted a very small number, are now quite numerous, as the Italian government is currently welcoming students from our country to study there. As for the subjects studied by these students, engineering and technology are more popular than social sciences, which is also a positive phenomenon.

(2) Establish a model primary school, and appoint He Shangping, Li Yingbiao, etc., as the preparatory committee. The start-up funds will be allocated from the association's cash fund, and the school site will be located in Shanghai. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Wang Xinmin, He Bingsong, and Others Publish a Declaration on Culture Construction Rooted in China (Part 1) 249

Wang Xinming, He Bingsong, Wu Yugan, Sun Hanbing, Huang Wenshan, Tao Xisheng, Zhang Yi, Chen Gaoyong, Fan Zhongyun, Sa Mengwu, and others have issued a declaration on culture construction rooted in China, stating:

1. China is Gone: In the realm of culture, we cannot see present-day China. China is in a dense fog, its form indistinct, in a severe cold where all things are curled up, with no light and no heat. In order to seek light and heat, Chinese people are suffering, groping, and struggling. Some are desperately burrowing into the tombs of the ancients, hoping to beg a little light and heat from the skeletons; others are clinging to the feet of European and American missionaries, hoping that the missionaries will lower a rope to save all living beings and hoist them up to the bright and warm heaven. But the skeletons are leading them from the edge of darkness to the depths of darkness, from the bleak late autumn into the frigid winter. The missionaries are suspending them in mid-air, causing them to drift, wander, yearn, and grope in a realm of emptiness where they cannot touch the sky above or the earth below. The result is the same disappointment. China has disappeared in the realm of culture. The form of Chinese politics, the organization of society, and the content and form of thought have lost their characteristics. The people nurtured by this uncharacteristic politics, society, and thought can no longer be considered Chinese. Therefore, we can confidently say that from the perspective of culture, China no longer exists in the modern world, and even within China's territory, there are almost no Chinese people left. To enable China to raise its head again in the realm of culture, and to ensure that Chinese politics, society, and thought all possess Chinese characteristics, we must engage in cultural construction rooted in China. Japanese painters often say, "Although Westerners dislike the excessively strong colors of Japanese paintings, if Japanese paintings did not have that glaringly strong color, how could they be Japanese paintings?" We also need to have such an understanding in cultural construction. To engage in cultural construction rooted in China, we must use a critical attitude and scientific methods to examine China's past, grasp China's present, and build China's future. We should make our greatest efforts in these three areas.

2. A Complete Reckoning: China once occupied a very important position in the realm of culture. From ancient times until the Qin and Han dynasties, it was in a process of upward progress. The Spring and Autumn and Warring States periods formed our Greek and Roman era, which was truly a flourishing period of Chinese culture. But after the Han dynasty, Chinese culture stagnated. Although the Song and Ming dynasties saw a new development, integrating indigenous Confucianism and Taoism with foreign Buddhism, it did not exceed the scope of past culture. Ultimately, it was something inherited. It was not until the Opium War that a major qualitative change occurred. Battleships and cannons brought news of Western culture, bringing a warning that threatened to lead China into a new era. Thus, the ancient culture was shaken, and we awakened from our inherited slumber. Accompanying this awakening was the "Westernization Movement" of Zeng Guofan and Li Hongzhang, the "Reform Movement" of Kang Youwei and Liang Qichao, and the "Revolutionary Movement" of Mr. Sun Yat-sen. Zeng and Li's Westernization Movement only knew the importance of "strong armor and sharp weapons" and "sound, light, chemistry, and electricity," which was entirely an imitation of technology. Kang and Liang's Reform Movement focused on legal reform to strengthen the country, which was merely a political plagiarism. These can all be said to be the view of "Chinese learning as the foundation, Western learning for practical use." Although it had its own historical mission of eliminating the old and establishing the new at the time, it was, after all, a superficial and reformist method that could not satisfy the demands of the time. Thus, there was the Xinhai Revolution led by Mr. Sun Yat-sen. He took the principle of "saving China's inherent things from the root" and "catching up with what others already have" as a prerequisite, advocating for a thorough reform of China's society, politics, and economy.

Zhongfa Industrial College Wins the Independent College Soccer Championship 255

Defeats Tongde Medical College 3-0

Yesterday, the rain cleared up, and the water puddles on the ground showed signs of drying. At 2:00 PM, the final of the Independent College Joint Sports Meet soccer championship was held. The participants in the final were Zhongfa Industrial College from Group A and Tongde Medical College from Group B, holding the closing game of the soccer tournament. The two sides clashed at the Jiaotong University soccer field. There were about a thousand cheerleaders and spectators present, which was the most spectacular situation of all the sports competitions. The players, amidst applause, entered the field one after another in high spirits, warming up and testing their foot skills. The referee blew the silver whistle, and the battle began. One was a famous iron army, and the other was a rising star. The drums and flags were evenly matched, and the swords and crossbows were drawn, killing each other. Soon, Zhongfa's right forward passed to the center forward, dribbling the ball forward. The Tongde defender blocked the charge, immediately turned and passed the ball to the center forward, dribbling it a few steps in the crowd, lifting his foot and shooting low, accurately, and quickly towards the left corner. The Tongde goalkeeper tried his best to block the shot, but the ball had already entered the net and could not be saved. After the defeat, Tongde launched a major offensive. The five forwards coordinated well, full of murderous intent, and their momentum was like breaking bamboo. But Zhongfa's front and back defenders were like copper walls and iron walls, densely arranged in a net, with strict defense, which really made it impossible for Tongde's forwards to take advantage of the gap. After a long time of such a melee, neither side gained anything, and the first half ended, with the battle temporarily suspended. Zhongfa won 1-0. After the break, Zhongfa continued to take advantage of the victory, with the right forward receiving the support of the forward and midfielder, protecting his position, and directly attacking the opponent's camp, scoring two more goals. Tongde refused to show weakness and ordered the three armies to kill into Zhongfa's interior. Unexpectedly, Zhongfa's right defender, due to excessive defense, touched the ball with his hand, and a penalty kick was awarded, which was kicked in by the Tongde center forward. A few minutes later, the whistle blew to stop the game. The final result was 3-0, a great victory for Zhongfa. The names and positions of Zhongfa's players are recorded below:

Lai ZhiQiu, Xie Gongliang, Lin Foxian, Cai Fuxiang, Yu Zongzhou, Chen Bingjun, Hu Mingkai, Hua Zurong, Xu Jinhai, He Xiaoyi, Ye Chuanfu.

Chronicles

Little Western Paradise 258

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter Seven: Hearing the Words, She Covers Her Tears and Sells Herself, Complaining of Hardship. Carefully Peering at the Invitation, She Earnestly Relies on Them.

Auntie Hu did not speak for a long time, then she replied, "Oh! How can he blame Master Cheng? Every word you say is what we poor people think. Other things are fake, but this is real." As she spoke, she held two silver dollars in her hand, bounced them up and down. Then she smiled and said, "The guests in this Little Western Paradise, there are upper, middle, and lower classes, right? Who would be willing to take out these shiny silver dollars to give to others?" Li Shilian understood completely at this time that it was Cheng Zhiqian who had shown a little kindness and touched the hearts of these two women. So he forced a smile and said, "There are many people who say good things these days, but few who do good deeds. Who wouldn't say a few good words? It's not easy to see someone giving silver dollars like this. If this young lady finds someone with a real heart like Mr. Cheng, then she will have a lifelong reliance." As he said this, he again assumed that hesitant attitude, holding a cigarette between two fingers and stretching it out to the side, tapping the middle finger on the cigarette, his eyes glancing at Yueying. Cheng Zhiqian raised his head and laughed heartily, "That's a joke. Using small favors to buy people's hearts, that's what Cao Cao and Wang Mang did. I gave these two dollars to Auntie Hu because I was afraid she would have such a misunderstanding. I had already stated in advance that she didn't need to talk to me about this young lady's affairs. I feel that when a person is born between heaven and earth, it is a very sad thing to repay someone's kindness with their body. If you give kindness to someone and hope that they will repay you with their body, that is causing them pain, which is ten times more hateful than not giving them kindness." Yueying was sitting on the side, and originally she had stopped crying. Hearing such thorough words, her heart was moved, and she started sobbing again. Zhiqian said, "You don't need to cry! Everyone has times when they are down on their luck. As long as you are patient and work slowly, sooner or later there will be a day when you get ahead. This Little Western Paradise, as Auntie Hu said, has upper, middle, and lower classes, it is a place of right and wrong. You should go back." (108)

The Discovery of the Jade Milk Well 259

— By Wang Shouqiu

The Jade Milk Well is a recent discovery in Nanjing. Just looking at the three characters "Jade Milk Well," we can tell that it is no ordinary ancient well!

The discovery happened like this: About ten li outside of Zhonghua Gate, there is Ande Gate, originally a Ming Dynasty outer city. Next to that city, there is a small earthen hill, which also has a fragrant name, called "Jade Ring Hill." On this hill, there are dozens of houses, all inhabited by farmers, and there is also a flowery temple, Xinglong Temple, which was also built in the Ming Dynasty. However, because it is relatively far from the city, people in the city rarely know about this place.

Recently, the abbot of Xinglong Temple, Jihang, saw a small dirt mound made of garbage behind the temple, which was really not very elegant, so he called a few villagers to move it away. Who knew that after leveling this small dirt mound, the "Jade Milk Well" was discovered! So Abbot Jihang spent a few more coins to remove the mud from the well, and thus this ancient well was completely revealed!

The Jade Milk Well is entirely built of alunite stone, and the patterns are very delicate. Above the well, the characters "Jade Milk Well" and "Rebuilt in the Fifteenth Year of Yongle" are engraved. The bottom of the well is also made of alunite stone, with several small holes on it in the style of plum blossoms. The well water emerges from these small holes, initially as very clear water, and then after a while, it turns into water that is the same as human milk! That's why it is called "Jade Milk Well." According to Abbot Jihang, the water tastes fragrant and sweet, and if it is used to brew tea, it is truly a unique flavor!

Seller of Chickens 261

— Drunken Simpleton

When winter arrives, in the streets and alleys, there are always villagers carrying loads on shoulder poles, calling out to sell chickens, to meet the needs of the residents.

The price of chickens is truly cheap this year: in previous years, one yuan could only buy two or three catties, but now one yuan can buy four or five catties (four catties for hens, five catties for roosters). And it's weighed on a full sixteen-tael scale. This is probably a manifestation of rural bankruptcy!

If you buy a few more of these cheap chickens, intending to raise them for future needs, you'll only be fooled and suffer a loss. Because these chickens often make strange noises after a day or two. Their combs also change from red to purplish-black, and they may even stop eating and moving. If you don't slaughter them at this time, they might just die of old age. But what's the reason for this? You only need to slaughter the chicken and cut it open to understand. Because its crop will be particularly swollen. The food inside is undigested, or mixed with mud and sand. This is the reason for its strange cries: these chicken vendors, to increase the weight of the chickens, stuff them with food in advance. They turn perfectly good chickens into a state of dying. These cruel methods are truly hateful. Now, the animal protection society initiated by philanthropists in this city is trying to protect all kinds of animals. For example, if someone carries a chicken upside down in the concession, if the police see it, they will be detained in the police station and punished. Compassion for animals can be said to be thorough. But the above-mentioned practice of forcibly stuffing chickens with food is still impossible to prohibit.

The Ethereal Records of Imperial Fragrance 262

— Originally Written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, Translated by Qin Shouou

"In the past, martial arts were very important! For a leader, in addition to handling all the government affairs of the court, hunting was also an important task that could not be neglected. It was necessary to hold it from time to time." The Empress Dowager was praising the ancestors' martial achievements again. As usual, we were all listening very attentively. When he went hunting, he brought a lot of people, because we Manchus never used hunting dogs when hunting, so he had to bring more people to help him search for wild animals. These wild animals - mostly tigers and leopards - were captured in advance, kept in large cages, and then released temporarily. ...

"Because this hunting ground is far from the city, the emperors were already very tired from riding all the way to get here, so they would definitely rest in this palace first; while he was resting, his entourage would be busy tidying up the horses, tightening the bowstrings, and sharpening all the arrowheads one by one. In addition, the precious sword that the emperor carried with him also had to be sharpened to maintain its sharpest state, so that it would not fail in case it was needed.

"You must know that the situation at that time was absolutely different from now: Manchus were all brave and fierce, strong and able to fight, and the most important thing was the spirit of martial arts; therefore, a leader who wants to rule his people cannot rely entirely on empty words or clever means, but must have a strong physique, be able to be familiar with martial arts, and be able to go to the battlefield. At the very least, he must not be weaker than any of his people; in other words, he must at least be as strong and brave as his people. (218)

Shen Bao Chunqiu Editorial Department

Looking Forward to the Arrival of Relief 264

— Moon

Random Talk

My Peach and Plum Calamity 265

— Late Evening Chamber Owner

(Preface) Recently, I saw a movie called "Peach and Plum Calamity," which is a tragedy of students. Moved by old events, I wrote it down as follows:

During the middle years of the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty, I pioneered the atmosphere in Guanzhong, such as newspapers and lectures, which were all my creations; and I especially devoted myself to primary school education, and the school I founded was named Gan Garden; at that time, the atmosphere had not yet opened up, and people called it "Foreign School"; however, in the first year of its start, the number of students who came to study had reached several hundreds, which was not easy; among them, there was a son of Mr. Zhou from Zhejiang, named Chengen, who was eleven years old. Mr. Zhou had a late-born son, who was intelligent and studious, and I loved him very much. He had an older sister who was several years older than Chengen, who was beautiful and intelligent, and also once asked my wife to teach her how to read; After more than a year, Mr. Zhou had a close relative who was an official in Fengxiang, and invited Mr. Zhou to assist in the government affairs. Mr. Zhou left his family in the provincial capital for his son's education, and went to the office alone. More than a year later, one day in school class, the roll call did not find Zhou Chengen. Just as I was about to send someone to ask about it, someone from Zhou's family came to ask for Chengen's sick leave. I felt uneasy. After class, I went to visit him and saw that his fever was very high. I told his family to pay special attention and report his recovery as soon as possible. After a few days, he did not come again. When asked, the illness was severe and dangerous, and he was talking nonsense, and he talked about school affairs a lot; and he occasionally said in his words: "Teacher Yan is here, you should entertain him quickly. ......" I felt sad when I heard it! I went to see him again and saw that his mind was confused. When he saw me coming, his eyes were piercing and he turned over to kowtow. My tears burst out! He died the next day. His mother and sister, considering that Mr. Zhou was old and only had this one son, were afraid of hurting his heart, so they went to Mr. Zhou's office and falsely said that they would leave their son in school and leave everything to me to take care of. After several years, his mother also died. Mr. Zhou felt that it was inconvenient for the father and daughter to live alone, so he took his daughter back to the province. As soon as the luggage was unloaded, his daughter secretly sent someone to tell me, and asked me to only say that Chengen had been sent to a certain school in Shanghai because he was very busy with his work and could not return immediately, and planned to send him abroad to study, intending to spend his father's remaining years in this way. After a while, Mr. Zhou came and thanked me earnestly, saying that he was deeply grateful for sending his son to Shanghai to study, and that he would ask about everything by registered mail; I did not answer because it was inconvenient, so I said yes. After a few days, his daughter came to my house gracefully, and said as soon as she entered the door: "I came to kowtow to the teacher and his wife especially," and then talked about Chengen, and asked again as before; and looked at my house back and forth, and asked about everything in detail, because my second son had just lost his wife at that time, and his father planned to propose marriage to my family. The next day, a matchmaker was sent to his house, but because I had not asked for my second son's consent, I could not agree immediately. At the meeting, Mr. Zhou's enemy knew about it and made slanderous remarks to my second son, and the young son was ignorant and fell into his trap! The marriage proposal was aborted. And Zhou's daughter suffered a serious illness due to disappointment. At that time, Mr. Zhou's letter sent to Shanghai was returned because there was no such school in Shanghai; Mr. Zhou spoke out and said, "Where did Yan put my son? He is deceiving me, I will sue him." The daughter was critically ill, and in a daze, she suddenly sobered up and said to her father generously: "I am critically ill and cannot get up! My brother Chengen died of a certain disease on a certain day of a certain year, and was buried in a certain place. The false statement about seeking knowledge is to keep the old father's heart at peace; this has nothing to do with the Yan family, so don't ask." After she finished speaking, she passed away. Mr. Zhou still thought it was a confused order in the illness, and after asking many old roommates, he believed it. The next day, Mr. Zhou came and said to me: "My son died early, and my family kept it from me. If my daughter had not told me directly before her death, I would have wronged you! "Later, Mr. Zhou, as an old man in his seventies, had no other worries, and returned to the south alone, and there was no news, and I don't know where he ended up.

Let's All Pick Up This Load Together 266

— Yang An

This year is the Student National Goods Year. Having the purest, most hardworking, and most patriotic students to do the work of promoting national goods and using national goods is, of course, the most appropriate and effective.

Silver flows in torrents, Foreign goods pour in,

How to stop the leakage? Work hard on national goods.

To save the panic of silver outflow, thousands of methods are not as effective and successful as working hard on promoting national goods and using national goods. Young students, from literate children to university students, and even old students who used to be students, should start from this year and enthusiastically engage in it. Mr. Huang Renzhi said: "I am also a member of the Student National Goods Year, because I have also been a student. The older I get, the better my enthusiasm." This spirit can be a model for our young people.

Chinese people should use Chinese goods,

From adults to children, from men to women,

Everyone should enthusiastically do it.

Don't let last year be the women's responsibility,

And this year only let the students do it.

As a result, you push me and I push you,

It must be a mess.

Originally, the so-called National Goods Year is just to mark a name to advocate the use of national goods by people all over the country. It does not mean that the National Goods Year of that sector only relies on the efforts of that sector and holds that sector responsible. Last year was "Women's National Goods Year," so did the men not have any responsibility and could use foreign goods? This year is "Student National Goods Year," so does it mean that the women's responsibility has been fulfilled and they don't have to use national goods anymore? I often say: this year is the first year of "Student National Goods Year," which is also the second year of "Women's National Goods Year," and the third year of "National Goods Year." Someone said well: everyone should recognize that this year is not just "Student National Goods Year," students should also use national goods. It is even more necessary to recognize that in "Student National Goods Year," it is not just those who are students who should use national goods. In short, using national goods and promoting national goods are the responsibility of everyone who is enthusiastic and everyone who is Chinese, and everyone must work hard. The opinions of many students below are enough for everyone to understand.

All Chinese people use Chinese goods, regardless of which year, work hard to move forward, children to adults, husbands to women, not you and me, not poor and rich, share the burden together, everyone is responsible.

The Future of the Student National Goods Year 267

— Zhang Zhizhong, Journalism Department, Shanghai University

The most unfortunate people in the world are those who are unfortunately mute and patients with paralysis, because although they have limbs and facial features, they cannot move freely and say what they want to say like normal healthy people.

It's really pitiful to say that our country, restricted by objective facts, has also become mute, an unfortunate paralytic:!! Leaving aside the great truth that enemies have occupied our territory by force, and we should recover it by force, other countries use long-term economic aggression as a means to control our lives, and trap us in the current terrible fact that the country is broken, the family is destroyed, the people are poor, and the wealth is exhausted, we can't even shout out the slogan of resisting goods, and the movement of resisting goods is also quite silent. Aren't we as unfortunate and pitiful as the mute and the paralytic?!! Although the annual "National Goods Year" is held in response to the needs of objective facts, it undertakes the work of increasing the production of national goods, reducing the import surplus of foreign goods, and resisting the dumping of foreign goods.

Last year was called "Women's National Goods Year." Women and national goods manufacturers also worked hard. National goods exhibitions were held in Shanghai, Hangzhou, Nanjing, Changsha, Yichang, and Xi'an. Fashion conferences were also performed in Shanghai, Nanjing, and other places. But what was the result? Japanese goods were still dumped in China in large quantities. The trade import surplus from January to October last year reached a huge 430 million yuan. And the crisis of national industries is becoming more and more acute. The silk industry has declined, and the textile industry has also declined. Other industries such as the rubber industry, match industry, cement industry, enamel industry, woolen industry, thermos bottle industry, oil production industry, and umbrella industry are still in the same depression.

Why?

This is, very obviously, under the shackles of unequal treaties and under the system where tariffs cannot be completely independent, the immature national industry is destroyed by the capitalism of the great powers with advanced capital and technology, and is forced to the desperate situation of exhaustion day by day.

However, national goods still need to be promoted after all, and national industries still need people to always love and protect them. If we wait until unequal treaties are lifted and tariffs are completely independent before we promote and protect them, then, capitalists from the East and the West may have already earned all the foreign money in our pockets! Our purchasing power is reduced to only enough to drink wind.

It is said that a monk asked: "How about taking three steps forward?" The answer is: "Bumping your head against the forehead!" "How about taking three steps back?" "A fall of a thousand feet!" "How about not advancing and not retreating?" "Die on the spot!"

The economic crisis we are suffering now is so serious and unavoidable. If we don't want to die and don't want to fall a thousand feet, then, we have to rush forward with our heads, and the way is: work hard for complete tariff autonomy, complete abolition of unequal treaties, and modernization and rational management of industry. Although this work may be head-scratching.

This year is the Student National Goods Year. Students, national goods manufacturers, and all the people, let us unite and work together!

Ten Commandments for the Student National Goods Year 268

— Tan Bingwen, National Shanghai College of Commerce

People at that time had a pessimistic view of the future of the national goods industry, which was due to the fact that the national goods movement was not promoted properly, and the effectiveness was also minimal. The National Goods Year has passed, and industry and commerce have become more and more depressed! The Women's National Goods Year has passed, and the import of foreign cosmetics, perfumes, and other women's products has not decreased compared to previous years, but has even increased! Learning from the past, we promote this year as the Student National Goods Year. If we are like in the past, those who promote it will promote it, and those who are involved will despise it, then the result can be predicted. Sad loss! The national spirit is so weak, can the future of China's national economy have hope of moving towards a bright realm? Our students are excellent members of the people, and the responsibility of national revival is placed on their shoulders. The rise of the national goods movement should begin with the Student National Goods Year.

After the war, Germany's industry and commerce declined internally, and was heavily in debt externally. It was not accidental that it completed economic recovery in a few years! This is probably because the German people's love of country is superior to other races. After the Germans suffered a disastrous defeat in the European war, they sought the revival of industry and commerce, and formulated the so-called "Ten Commandments of Industry," and the revitalization of the national goods industry depended on this. With the failure of past national goods movements in mind, I have exhausted my foolish sincerity and drafted the Ten Commandments of the Student National Goods Year after several deliberations to show my comrades. Its text is;

(1) National stationery is both cheap and beautiful. All my students should try their best to advocate its use.

(2) Physical education can strengthen the body, and using national sports equipment can save the country.

(3) Before your body loses its freedom, you should wear national clothing.

(4) Eating domestic products can cultivate patriotism.

(5) If you have a penny, you must deposit it in a domestic bank.

(6) When you travel, do not take foreign merchant ships.

(7) When you watch movies, do not enter foreign cinemas, and do not watch foreign films.

(8) Every time you spend a penny, you must take the welfare of the country as your guide.

(9) You must persuade your relatives and friends to use national goods every day.

(10) You must reflect on yourself every day whether you have violated the "Ten Commandments of National Goods"

Today, China's national industry and commerce are on the verge of exhaustion. Even in Shanghai, which is the most prosperous in the country, factories that have stopped work account for almost half of the total, and several shops close down every day. If this continues, what will happen? Saving the country and seeking survival, promoting national goods is the most urgent task. We are all outstanding students, and in the past we were known as traitors to national goods. Today, we should work hard to encourage ourselves to atone for our sins. Germany's past can be learned from, and we are already too late to catch up. Alas! Following the old ways and sticking to the old ways will only lead to self-destruction. It is time to drastically change our past mistakes and vigorously whip the horse at night to save ourselves. I urge my comrades not to ignore my words

— Ms. Hou Wanru, Jinling Women's University

At that time, the students opposed it. But the school authorities did not agree, and there was a regulation that "not wearing school uniforms will be regarded as absenteeism."

Do women in society want to be fishmongers or tailors? No, that's because people in society admire students and imitate them. Therefore, we believe that the clothing of female students, especially university students, has a great influence on social customs. Sisters! Why don't we use this kind of power? On the one hand, we can save our fathers and brothers' money, and on the other hand, we are good students who use national goods. Sisters! We are standing on the upper layer of the intellectual class, and we all have considerable national concepts. From now on, we will correct the bad habit of using foreign goods if we have it, and encourage ourselves if we don't have it, so as not to fail the expectations of society for us

— Yu Bailu, Nanyang Middle School

The past Women's National Goods Year gave us a historical lesson: the so-called ×× National Goods Year was the year ×× got scolded. Similarly, this year is when our students will be scolded. Students have never been able to clearly recognize shame. They think it is shameful to buy domestic goods, but they have never thought that buying British, American, etc. goods is equally shameful. They think that certain foreign shops should never be entered. Even when they have to buy a foreign book, they are still afraid of being seen by others, secretly sneaking into the ×× bookstore, and then quickly slipping out. Using this "lousy domestic product" is shameful, so they hide it.

We originally have the power, we originally have brains. Friends, on New Year's Eve this year (no, not just this year), let's see our achievements.

Investigation of Daily Necessities of College and Middle School Students 272

— Ying Geng, Sino-French Vocational School

This year is the Student National Goods Year. In order to do some practical work this year, I investigated the daily necessities of many college and middle school students. The result is that 60-70% of them are foreign goods. The most common ones are:

Stationery! Ink, fountain pens. Most students use Waterman American ink, and fountain pens are Conklin, Parker, Cade, etc. National goods ink includes Dahua, Minsheng, Liwen, etc., and national goods fountain pens include Guan Le Min, Xinmin, Huafu, etc., but they are still no match for the popularity of foreign goods.

Instruments. We rarely see national goods instruments. Most of the ones they use are produced by the German Faber factory.

Sports equipment, musical instruments! In their spare time, middle school and college students have to play sports or music, but the sports equipment such as tennis rackets, baseball bats, football shoes, running shoes, jumping shoes, etc., and the various Western musical instruments they use are all foreign goods.

Other items such as toothpaste, belts, suits, hats, shoes, gloves, etc. are mostly foreign goods as well.

It has become a habit for middle school and college students to use foreign goods. They seem ashamed to use domestic goods. The reasons are: (1) a lack of trust in the concept of domestic goods; (2) differences in the material of foreign goods and domestic goods, such as instruments and stationery, domestic goods really cannot make people fully believe; (3) most middle school and college students are children of the bourgeoisie, and they have developed the habit of using foreign goods in their families since childhood; (4) a mentality of vanity.

Remedial methods are nothing more than: (1) establishing greater factories and producing more refined and accurate products; (2) organizing promotion of national goods and review committees within schools; (3) organizing consumer cooperatives to exclusively sell excellent American goods, so that students can avoid the trouble of shopping outside and can purchase national goods; (4) publicizing the advantages of national goods; (5) rewarding the solicitation of students to provide ways for national goods manufacturers to improve their products, etc.

Personal opinions are certainly not necessarily correct, and I hope that all parties will discuss them as much as possible.

Student National Goods Year and Stationery 273

— Pan Yinge

The 24th year of the Republic of China is officially designated as the Student National Goods Year. The Student National Goods Year will certainly have its great manifestations. However, in this article, I want to raise a small topic, which is the stationery used by students.

The stationery of the Student National Goods Year is like the脂粉of the Women's National Goods Year. Women's脂粉has already attracted the attention of many people. We must advocate for national goods in the stationery used by students, and at the same time, use less foreign goods and no inferior goods.

First, let's talk about advocating for national goods. Take the author himself as an example. I myself must use Chinese stationery for my writing. I have translated an average of one book per year for the past two years. The manuscript paper I use is Chinese毛邊, Huizhou ink, and Huzhou brush. The stationery and envelopes I use to correspond with friends are also domestic goods. I feel that they are very elegant and very respectful to people. Some people often use foreign paper for writing manuscripts, which is not right. As for using foreign envelopes and foreign stationery to correspond with people, it feels even more disrespectful.

Second, let's talk about using less foreign goods. It is impossible to completely abolish foreign goods in stationery. For example, when traveling and conducting investigations, it is convenient to take notes at any time, so it is of course convenient to use pencils. However, it can be said that there are no domestic goods pencils, so foreign goods cannot be avoided. But it can certainly be used less. For example, you can use a毛筆when drafting indoors. Now students like to use foreign goods. Even when they can avoid it, they still happily use foreign goods. During this Student National Goods Year, I sincerely hope that they will change their approach.

Third, let's talk about not using inferior goods. Nowadays, some students love foreign goods, but they also dislike their high prices, so they choose to buy cheap stationery, and unknowingly use inferior goods. In fact, it is better not to buy them if you dislike the price. For example, you don't necessarily have to buy expensive fountain pens. But you should not buy cheap ones either. That's why I don't like this thing myself. I am always looking forward to China having a good fountain pen factory.

My Experience in Promoting National Goods 275

— Qu Kaixi, School of Commerce, Great China University

For our country with backward production, promoting national goods has become a unanimous good method for saving the country and preserving its existence. For a nation to exist permanently in the world, its products must have the ability to be self-sufficient. Promoting national goods is to encourage the production of products and is bound to become a way to be self-sufficient. Based on this importance, I enthusiastically participate in the work, but it is definitely not a general empty promise. Below are the results of promoting my use and promotion of national goods: (A) Factors that promote the use of national goods:

(1) A good family that promotes national goods. My parents have received new education and baptism. They have a broad vision and full understanding, so their family education; for children's psychology, first of all, national goods are beautiful, and the habit of practical use is formed. Almost all daily necessities at home are first adopted with national goods as a prerequisite. Therefore, my brothers and sisters and I have developed my good habit of using national goods.

(2) The influence of the school atmosphere: Dr. Tai Shuangqiu, the dean of the School of Education of this school, advocates the土布movement, and many students participate in it. This has formed the simple style of the school. In this environment, I wear uniforms every day, which makes me energetic, convenient for work, and physically strong, while the expenses borne by the family are greatly reduced.

(B) Practice of promoting national goods:

(1) Introduce exquisite national goods to relatives and friends: When my family and I give gifts to relatives and friends for weddings and funerals, we give national goods or gift certificates from national goods companies. This way, we send them to them, so that they have a correct understanding of national goods and arouse their awareness.

(2) Correcting the wrong concepts with words: Since the Chinese people do not have a proper understanding of national goods, it is of course easy to have wrong views. Therefore, I often introduce the advantages of national goods in women's characters and contribute opinions on promotion:

1. Introduce the fineness and benefits of using national goods to people in the society.

2. Contribute opinions on the production of practical products to factories.

3. Correct and remedy the situation where an employee of a certain national goods company uses a foreign lead pencil (Chicken brand) instead of the national Dahua pencil.

4. Advocates that schools should wear uniforms to reduce the burden on families and to prevent students from entering舞塲and going to improper amusement塲.

The above is my good environment that promotes my use of national goods, and my experience in promoting national goods. This year is the Student National Goods Year. I hope that the督促of the論, the rewards and punishments of the government's education authorities, the preferential treatment of manufacturers, and the close connection between families and schools will monitor students to thoroughly use national goods. At the same time, I hope that students across the country will consciously and forever use national goods. We must know that using foreign goods is the most shameful thing!

US Cotton Market Conditions Show Obvious Improvement 287

Cotton Board Inflow Gradually Decreasing

Worldwide Cotton Production Further Reduced

Washington, 8th: Johnston, manager of the Cotton Board, announced today that the current stock of spot cotton is 1,617,932 bales, and the cotton futures for May, July, and October are 20,900 bales. According to Johnston's opinion, at the current market price, cotton holders are unlikely to have a large number of cotton certificates flowing into the Cotton Board, and the average daily inflow has recently decreased by 200 bales. Washington, 8th: The worldwide cotton production in 1934, as estimated by the US Department of Agriculture's Bureau of Economics, is 23,000,000 bales, a decrease of 200,000 bales from the November estimate and a decrease of 3,100,000 bales from the 1933 production.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, more than ten sources from various inland groups arrived at the Hexia wharf, with about 200 ships stored in the river. In terms of market sales, although the weather had cleared in Tiangong, Bai Chang was still being sold. There were many inquiries about pushing Yangjian. The market shape was that high-end white japonica rice was fixed, and medium and lower grades were fatigued by a small number of points. The price of thin rice was close to 0.1 lower. The price of Yangjian was strong. There was not much increase or decrease in Bianyuan Du wharf guest rice.

Foreign Rice Suddenly Falls by 0.1 to 0.2 in the Afternoon 293

Guest Xiang Arrives in Small Quantities and Stays Flat; Foreign Rice Returns and Sales are Competitive

Yesterday, the market situation for Guest Xiang was that inland demand was weak, but demand in this street was still strong, and there were inquiries from Chongsha, so the market could stand relatively firm. More than 3,000 bags were sold citywide, and most of them were handled by Yamamoto Street. More than 50,000 bags of foreign rice were newly imported by the Freighter Freck ship (this ship was delayed due to wind resistance last time). New arrivals were still arriving on the same day, and market sentiment had already become weak. The merchants who had purchased in the previous days were also eager to sell. Because the market had been active based on this guest last time, the market could stand relatively firm. In the afternoon, all parties sold back, and foreign merchants also had 500 tons of new transactions, so the market immediately fell sharply. The opening selling price for April Saigon was 5 yuan in the morning, and it dropped to 4.89 yuan in the afternoon, but there were still no buyers. If the inflow of merchants is not strong now and tomorrow, it will still need to step down. The opening price for January Saigon was 4.85 yuan in the morning, and there were no inquiries at 4.75 yuan in the afternoon. The spot price for Saigon fell to 11 yuan in the afternoon, and the market shape was still shaky.

Oil Market - White Tung Oil Foreign Sales Uninterrupted 294

Since the end of the year, the Hankou market sold white tung oil to foreign merchants at 31 yuan per dan according to foreign regulations. In the first three or four days of the New Year, because foreign firms stopped trading, the market has been unchanged in recent days, and trading has continued at the same price. However, the first month's futures that were previously sold short have reached their delivery period, and most of them are delivered in the producing areas. Therefore, the arrival of goods in Hankou is extremely rare. Only a few hundred pieces of Xiangtung were opened at a price of about 26 yuan. However, because too many futures were sold short to foreign firms, there is a delivery period every month, so the source in Hankou in the future is unlikely to surge in, and the market is also not easy to become too cheap. For this reason, the situation is very stable. The business of foreign merchants in this port is also continuously uninterrupted, but they are all small numbers of retail sales, and the market rarely pays attention. Recently, a certain miscellaneous grain store, which has always been engaged in exporting tung oil, has heard of finishing sufficient goods in Hangzhou at a price of 26.4 yuan per load, with shipping included. There should be a market for them, and the previously sold short futures have probably reached their delivery period. From this point of view, it is also difficult for Zhejiang tung to return to small size. However, domestic sales are quiet, and the settlement period is approaching in an instant, so people are more likely to wait and see.

Hardware - Hardware Transactions Gradually Clear 298

Hardware transactions are approaching the end of the year, and there is no big business. Such as British steel plate, galvanized iron, garden wire, cut iron, new lead wire, etc., all go downstream, so the price has fallen by 0.05 to 0.12. However, Hunan pure antimony is still in short supply, so the market price is still as high as 850 yuan, but there are not many transactions. Only the investigation yesterday showed that the goods opened on the market included 200 barrels of nails, more than 140 boxes of tinplate, 50 pieces of angle iron, more than 100 dan of blue lead, 230-40 bundles of galvanized iron sheet, 300 dan of new foreign yuan, more than 30 dan of tin solder, and 310 bundles of black iron sheet. Although there are other openings, many are small. The buyers were found to be the Yangtze River, inland river, and Fuzhou groups. The Tianjin, Yantai, and Qingdao groups have not heard of any transactions this week.
